Topic: Minecraft ### Response:  Question: A player has 12000 experience points. Experience points are earned by killing monsters. 
Each monster drops 100 experience points. 
How many monsters does the player have to kill to get 12000 experience points?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The player has 12000 experience points
    experience_points = 12000
    #Each monster drops 100 experience points
    experience_per_monster = 100
    #The answer is
    monsters = experience_points / experience_per_monster
    return monsters
Topic: Hello Kitty ### Response:  Question: Hello Kitty has 500 pencils. 200 of the pencils are blue, 150 of the pencils are pink, and the rest are green. How many green pencils does Hello Kitty have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Hello Kitty has 500 pencils
    total_pencils = 500
    #200 of the pencils are blue
    blue_pencils = 200
    #150 of the pencils are pink
    pink_pencils = 150
    #The rest are green. The answer is
    green_pencils = total_pencils - blue_pencils - pink_pencils
    return green_pencils

Topic: Serena Williams ### Response:  Question: Serena Williams has 200 trophies. 100 of them are tennis trophies. 70 of them are from the Australian Open. 30 of them are from the US Open.  How many trophies does Serena have that are not from the Australian Open or the US Open?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total trophies
    total_trophies = 200
    #Trophies from the Australian Open
    trophies_aus_open = 70
    #Trophies from the US Open
    trophies_us_open = 30
    #Trophies not from the Australian Open or the US Open
    trophies_not_aus_us = total_trophies - trophies_aus_open - trophies_us_open
    return trophies_not_aus_us

Topic: dogs ### Response:  Question: 10,000 dogs are barking. 1/4 of the dogs are Rottweilers. 1/5 of the Rottweilers are friendly. How many friendly Rottweilers are there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total dogs
    total_dogs = 10000
    #Rottweilers are 1/4 of the dogs
    rottweilers = total_dogs * 1/4
    #Among the Rottweilers, friendly ones are 1/5
    friendly_rottweilers = rottweilers * 1/5
    #The answer is
    result = friendly_rottweilers
    return result
Topic: Barbie ### Response:  Question: 300 Barbie dolls were in a toy store. 120 of the dolls were pink, 60 of the dolls were blue, and the rest were yellow. How many of the dolls were yellow?
Solution:
def solution():
    #300 Barbie dolls were in a toy store
    dolls_total = 300
    #120 of the dolls were pink
    dolls_pink = 120
    #60 of the dolls were blue
    dolls_blue = 60
    #The rest were yellow
    dolls_yellow = dolls_total - dolls_pink - dolls_blue
    return dolls_yellow

def solution():

    cheerleaders_per_side = 4

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: There are 100 scoops of ice cream in a 1000-scoop cone. 
Solution:
def solution():
    #There are 100 scoops of ice cream in a 1000-scoop cone
    scoops_in_cone = 1000
    #100 scoops is 10% of 1000
    scoops_percentage = 100 / 1000
    #The answer is
    result = scoops_in_cone * scoops_percentage
    return result
Topic: Captain America ### Response:  Question: Captain America has 2000 shields. He deploys 200 shields in each of the 10 states. How many shields does he have left?
Solution: 
def solution():
    #Captain America has 2000 shields
    shields_total = 2000
    #He deploys 200 shields in each of the 10 states
    shields_per_state = 200
    #There are 10 states
    states = 10
    #The answer is
    result = shields_total - shields_per_state * states
    return result

Topic: LeBron James ### Response:  Question: LeBron James, the NBA superstar, has 5000 points. He has 1000 more points than the next highest scorer. How many points does the next highest scorer have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #LeBron James has 5000 points
    lebron_points = 5000
    #The next highest scorer has 1000 less than LeBron
    next_highest_scorer_points = lebron_points - 1000
    #The answer is
    result = next_highest_scorer_points
    return result

Topic: dogs ### Response:  Question: There are 12 dogs in the dog park. 6 of the dogs are beagles. 3 of the dogs are dachshunds. 2 of the dogs are pugs. 1 of the dogs is a corgi. How many of the dogs are not the listed breeds?
Solution:
def solution():
    #There are 12 dogs in the dog park
    total_dogs = 12
    #6 of the dogs are beagles
    beagles = 6
    #3 of the dogs are dachshunds
    dachshunds = 3
    #2 of the dogs are pugs
    pugs = 2
    #1 of the dogs is a corgi
    corgi = 1
    #The answer is
    result = total_dogs - beagles - dachshunds - pugs - corgi
    return result
Topic: trains ### Response:  Question: 1000 people are in a train. 200 of them are in the first class, 300 of them are in the second class, and the rest are in the third class. How many people are in the third class?
Solution:
def solution():
    # Total people in the train
    total_people = 1000
    # People in the first class
    first_class = 200
    # People in the second class
    second_class = 300
    # The rest of the people are in the third class
    third_class = total_people - first_class - second_class
    return third_class
Topic: Wonder Woman ### Response:  Question: 10000 people lined up to buy ice cream. 8000 of them bought a scoop of ice cream, 2000 of them bought two scoops, and 1000 of them bought three scoops. 200 people left the line. How many people bought ice cream?
Solution:
def solution():
    #10000 people lined up
    people_lined_up = 10000
    #8000 of them bought a scoop of ice cream
    scoop_1 = 8000
    #2000 of them bought two scoops
    scoop_2 = 2000
    #1000 of them bought three scoops
    scoop_3 = 1000
    #200 people left the line
    people_left = 200
    #The answer is
    result = people_lined_up - people_left
    return result

Topic: candy ### Response:  Question: 600 candy bars were in a box. 200 more candy bars were added. 50 candy bars were taken out. How many candy bars are in the box now?
Solution:
def solution():
    #600 candy bars were in a box
    candy_bars_initial = 600
    #200 more candy bars were added
    candy_bars_added = 200
    #50 candy bars were taken out
    candy_bars_taken = 50
    #The answer is
    result = candy_bars_initial + candy_bars_added - candy_bars_taken
    return result

Topic: soccer ### Response:  Question: There were 16 participants in a soccer skills challenge. 

5 of the participants were from the 1st grade.

6 of the participants were from the 2nd grade.

2 of the participants were from the 3rd grade.

3 of the participants were from the 4th grade.

How many participants were from grades greater than 4?
Solution:
def solution():

    # total participants

    total_participants = 16

    # participants from 1st grade

    participants_1st_grade = 5

    # participants from 2nd grade

    participants_2nd_grade = 6

    # participants from 3rd grade

    participants_3rd_grade = 2

    # participants from 4th grade

    participants_4th_grade = 3

    # participants from grades greater than 4

    participants_greater_than_4 = total_participants - participants_1st_grade - participants_2nd_grade - participants_3rd_grade - participants_4th_grade

    return participants_greater_than_4
Topic: Fortnite ### Response:  Question: There are 200 players in a Fortnite match. 50 of them are from the US. 20 of them are from the UK. 40 of them are from Canada. 20 of them are from Australia. 10 of them are from Germany. How many of them are from other countries?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total players
    total_players = 200
    #US players
    us_players = 50
    #UK players
    uk_players = 20
    #Canada players
    canada_players = 40
    #Australia players
    australia_players = 20
    #Germany players
    germany_players = 10
    #Other countries players
    other_countries_players = total_players - (us_players + uk_players + canada_players + australia_players + germany_players)
    #The answer is
    result = other_countries_players
    return result

Topic: Ninja Turtles ### Response: 4 Ninja Turtles, Leonardo, Raphael, Donatello, and Michelangelo are practicing their katas. Leonardo does 15 push-ups, Raphael does 20, Donatello does 25, and Michelangelo does 30. How many push-ups do they do in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Leonardo does 15 push-ups
    leonardo_pushups = 15
    #Raphael does 20
    raphael_pushups = 20
    #Donatello does 25
    donatello_pushups = 25
    #Michelangelo does 30
    michelangelo_pushups = 30
    #The answer is
    result = leonardo_pushups + raphael_pushups + donatello_pushups + michelangelo_pushups
    return result
Topic: Black Panther ### Response:  Question: Black Panther can sneak into 50 Vibranium vaults in 3 minutes. How many can he sneak into in 4 hours?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Black Panther can sneak into 50 Vibranium vaults in 3 minutes
    vaults_per_minute = 50 / 3
    #4 hours is 240 minutes
    minutes = 4 * 60
    #The answer is
    result = vaults_per_minute * minutes
    return result

Topic: lacrosse ### Response:  Question: 4 lacrosse teams are playing in a tournament. Each team has 12 players. The 1st and 2nd place teams will play in the finals. How many players will be in the finals?
Solution:
def solution():
    #4 lacrosse teams
    num_teams = 4
    #Each team has 12 players
    num_players_per_team = 12
    #The 1st and 2nd place teams will play in the finals
    num_finals_teams = 2
    #The number of players in the finals is
    num_players_finals = num_finals_teams * num_players_per_team
    return num_players_finals
Topic: dinosaurs ### Response:  Question: A T-Rex is 50 feet long, and a Brontosaurus is 15 feet long. 2 T-Rexes and 4 Brontosauruses are in a movie. How long are the dinosaurs in the movie?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A T-Rex is 50 feet long
    t_rex_length = 50
    #A Brontosaurus is 15 feet long
    brontosaurus_length = 15
    #2 T-Rexes and 4 Brontosauruses are in a movie
    t_rex_count = 2
    brontosaurus_count = 4
    #The total length of the dinosaurs in the movie is
    result = (t_rex_length * t_rex_count) + (brontosaurus_length * brontosaurus_count)
    return result
Topic: Serena Williams ### Response:  Question: In 2017, Serena Williams won 10 Grand Slam titles. In 2018, she won 15. In 2019, she won 20. How many Grand Slam titles has she won in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #In 2017, she won 10 Grand Slam titles
    grand_slam_titles_2017 = 10
    #In 2018, she won 15
    grand_slam_titles_2018 = 15

    grand_slam_titles_2019 = 20
    #The answer is

    return result

Topic: Super Mario ### Response:  Question: Super Mario has 500 coins. He has to use 100 coins to get into the Mushroom Kingdom. He has to use 200 coins to get the Fire Flower. He has to use 300 coins to get the Star. How many coins does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Super Mario has 500 coins
    coins_initial = 500
    #He uses 100 coins to get into the Mushroom Kingdom
    coins_mushroom_kingdom = 100
    #He uses 200 coins to get the Fire Flower
    coins_fire_flower = 200
    #He uses 300 coins to get the Star
    coins_star = 300
    #Coins left
    coins_left = coins_initial - coins_mushroom_kingdom - coins_fire_flower - coins_star
    return coins_left
Topic: Fortnite ### Response:  Question: In Fortnite, 120 players are in a match. 10 players are eliminated in the first round. 20 more players are eliminated in the second round. 30 players are eliminated in the third round. How many players are left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #120 players are in a match
    players_initial = 120
    #10 players are eliminated in the first round
    players_eliminated_first_round = 10
    #20 more players are eliminated in the second round
    players_eliminated_second_round = 20
    #30 players are eliminated in the third round
    players_eliminated_third_round = 30
    #The answer is
    result = players_initial - players_eliminated_first_round - players_eliminated_second_round - players_eliminated_third_round
    return result

Topic: Patrick Mahomes ### Response:  Question: Patrick Mahomes has 4000 passing yards. 
He passes for 300 yards a game. 
He has played 10 games. 
How many more passing yards does he need to break the record of 5000 passing yards in a season?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Patrick Mahomes has 4000 passing yards
    passing_yards_initial = 4000
    #He passes for 300 yards a game
    yards_per_game = 300
    #He has played 10 games
    games_played = 10
    #The record is 5000 passing yards
    record = 5000
    #The answer is
    result = record - passing_yards_initial - (yards_per_game * games_played)
    return result
Topic: Hello Kitty ### Response:  Question: Hello Kitty has 10 pencils, 5 erasers, and 15 notebooks. 3 of the pencils are pink, 3 of the erasers are pink, and 4 of the notebooks are pink. How many pink school supplies does Hello Kitty have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Hello Kitty has 10 pencils, 5 erasers, and 15 notebooks
    total_pencils = 10
    total_erasers = 5
    total_notebooks = 15
    #3 of the pencils are pink, 3 of the erasers are pink, and 4 of the notebooks are pink. The answer is
    pink_supplies = 3 * 0.3 * total_pencils + 3 * 0.6 * total_erasers + 4 * 0.25 * total_notebooks
    return pink_supplies

Topic: Super Mario ### Response:  Question: There are 200 coins in a mushroom house. 150 of them are 1-coin coins, and the rest are 5-coin coins. How many 5-coin coins are there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of coins
    total_coins = 200
    #Number of 1-coin coins
    one_coin_coins = 150
    #Number of 5-coin coins is
    five_coin_coins = total_coins - one_coin_coins
    return five_coin_coins
Topic: Minecraft ### Response:  Question: Steve has 1000 experience points. He needs 200 to get to the next level. He also needs to get 200 to enchant an item. He enchanters an item 5 times. How many experience points does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Steve started with 1000 experience points
    experience_initial = 1000
    #He needed 200 to get to the next level
    experience_next_level = 200
    #He also needed 200 to enchant an item
    experience_enchant = 200
    #He enchanted an item 5 times
    enchantment_times = 5
    #Each enchantment cost 40 experience points
    experience_per_enchant = 40
    #He earned from enchanting
    experience_gained = enchantment_times * experience_per_enchant
    #The answer is
    experience_left = experience_initial - experience_next_level - experience_enchant - experience_gained
    return experience_left

Topic: Thor, the God of Thunder ### Response:  Question:  Thor, the God of Thunder, has 1000 thunderbolts.  He hurls 100 thunderbolts at the Midgard Serpent, 200 at the Frost Giants, and 300 at the Dark Elves.  How many thunderbolts does he have left?
def solution():
    #Thor has 1000 thunderbolts
    thunderbolts_initial = 1000
    #He hurls 100 thunderbolts at the Midgard Serpent
    thunderbolts_midgard = 100
    #200 at the Frost Giants
    thunderbolts_frost = 200
    #300 at the Dark Elves
    thunderbolts_dark = 300
    #The answer is
    result = thunderbolts_initial - thunderbolts_midgard - thunderbolts_frost - thunderbolts_dark
    return result

    #1 point is awarded for every save made by the goalie

    #1 point is awarded for every ground ball recovered
    points_per_ground_ball = 1

    goals_first_team = 5
    #The second team scored 3 goals
    goals_second_team = 3
    #The first team made 3 saves
    saves_first_team = 3
    #The second team made 5 saves
    saves_second_team = 5
    #The first team recovered 4 ground balls
    ground_balls_first_team = 4
    #The second team recovered 2 ground balls
    ground_balls_second_team = 2
    #The first team has a total of
    total_points_first_team = points_per_goal * goals_first_team + points_per_save * saves_first_team + points_per_ground_ball * ground_balls_first_team
    #The second team has a total of
    total_points_second_team = points_per_goal * goals_second

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: 
Alice and Bob go to the ice cream shop. Alice buys 2 scoops of the $3 a scoop peach ice cream. Bob buys 3 scoops of the $2 a scoop chocolate ice cream. How much more money does Alice spend?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Alice buys 2 scoops of the $3 a scoop peach ice cream
    alice_peach = 2 * 3
    #Bob buys 3 scoops of the $2 a scoop chocolate ice cream
    bob_chocolate = 3 * 2
    #The answer is
    result = alice_peach - bob_chocolate
    return result
Topic: field hockey ### Response: 11 players on a field hockey team. A field hockey team needs 1 goalie, 2 defenders, and 3 midfielders. How many forward players do they have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #11 players on a field hockey team
    players = 11
    #1 goalie
    goalie = 1
    #2 defenders
    defenders = 2
    #3 midfielders
    midfielders = 3
    #The answer is
    result = players - goalie - defenders - midfielders
    return result

Topic: Pokémon ### Response:  Question:  Charmander, Squirtle, and Bulbasaur are all Pokémon. Charmander is 20 years old, Squirtle is 25 years old, and Bulbasaur is 30 years old. How old is the average Pokémon?
Solution:

def solution():
    #Charmander is 20 years old
    charmander_age = 20
    #Squirtle is 25 years old
    squirtle_age = 25
    #Bulbasaur is 30 years old
    bulbasaur_age = 30
    #The answer is
    result = (charmander_age + squirtle_age + bulbasaur_age) / 3
    return result

Topic: Minecraft ### Response:  Question: Steve has 4000 experience points. 1000 of them are from mining, 1500 of them are from fighting, and 500 of them are from enchanting. How many of them are from crafting?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Steve has 4000 experience points
    experience_points_total = 4000
    #1000 of them are from mining
    experience_points_mining = 1000
    #1500 of them are from fighting
    experience_points_fighting = 1500
    #500 of them are from enchanting
    experience_points_enchanting = 500
    #The rest are from crafting. The answer is
    experience_points_crafting = experience_points_total - experience_points_mining - experience_points_fighting - experience_points_enchanting
    return experience_points_crafting

The rest of the Pokémon were Snorlax. How many Snorlax were there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A total of 1000 Pokémon were seen
    total_pokemon = 1000
    #200 of the Pokémon were Pikachu
    pikachu = 200
    #300 of the Pokémon were Squirtle
    squirtle = 300
    #400 of the Pokémon were Charmander
    charmander = 400
    #400 of the Pokémon were Bulbasaur
    bulbasaur = 400
    #300 of the Pokémon were Jigglithop
    jigglithop = 300
    #The rest of the Pokémon were Snorlax
    snorlax = total_pokemon - pikachu - squirtle - charmander - bulbasaur - jigglithop

Topic: Thor, the God of Thunder ### Response:  Question: Thor has 1000 thunderbolts. He uses 100 thunderbolts to battle Loki, and 100 more to battle the Frost Giants. How many thunderbolts does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Thor has 1000 thunderbolts
    thunderbolts_initial = 1000
    #He uses 100 thunderbolts to battle Loki
    thunderbolts_used_loki = 100
    #and 100 more to battle the Frost Giants
    thunderbolts_used_frost_giants = 100
    #Thunderbolts left is
    thunderbolts_left = thunderbolts_initial - thunderbolts_used_loki - thunderbolts_used_frost_giants
    #The answer is
    result = thunderbolts_left
    return result

5. Red Ranger + Blue Ranger + Yellow Ranger + Pink Ranger + Green Ranger + Gold Ranger + White Ranger + Mega Red Ranger (Red Ranger + Red Ranger + Red Ranger) + Mega Red Ranger (Red Ranger + Red Ranger + Red Ranger) * 2 = 10 + 20 + 30 + 40 + 50 + 60 + 70 + 30 + 60 = 370.

Topic: unicorns ### Response:  Question: A unicorn ate 30 dandelions and 12 blueberries. If dandelions have 10 calories and blueberries have 5 calories, how many calories did the unicorn eat?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The unicorn ate 30 dandelions
    dandelions = 30
    #Each dandelion has 10 calories
    dandelion_calories = 10
    #The unicorn ate 12 blueberries
    blueberries = 12
    #Each blueberry has 5 calories
    blueberry_calories = 5
    #The total calories are
    total_calories = (dandelions * dandelion_calories) + (blueberries * blueberry_calories)
    return total_calories

Topic: football ### Response:  Question: In a game, 20 players on each team scored 1 point. 

How many total points were scored in the game?
Solution:
def solution():
    #20 players on each team
    players_per_team = 20
    #Each player scored 1 point
    points_per_player = 1
    #There are 2 teams
    number_of_teams = 2
    #The total number of players is
    total_players = players_per_team * number_of_teams
    #The total number of points is
    total_points = total_players * points_per_player
    return total_points

Topic: Iron Man ### Response:  Question: Iron Man is a superhero who flies a high-tech suit. He has 24 armor suits. He flies 3 suits a day. How many days will it take to fly all of them?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man has 24 armor suits
    suits = 24
    #He flies 3 suits a day
    suits_per_day = 3
    #The answer is
    result = suits / suits_per_day
    return result
Topic: Batman ### Response: 2021 Batman: The Dark Knight Returns. Batman is a superhero. He is 5.5 feet tall and weighs 220 pounds. He can bench press 500 pounds. 2021's Batman is 2.5 feet taller and 20 pounds heavier than 2020's Batman. How many more pounds can 2021's Batman bench press than 2020's Batman?
Solution:
def solution():
    #2021 Batman is 5.5 feet tall and weighs 220 pounds
    height_2021 = 5.5
    weight_2021 = 220
    #2021's Batman can bench press 500 pounds
    bench_press_2021 = 500
    #2021's Batman is 2.5 feet taller and 20 pounds heavier than 2020's Batman
    height_diff = 2.5
    weight_diff = 20
    #2020 Batman is
    height_2020 = height_2021 - height_diff
    weight_2020 = weight_2021 - weight_diff
    #2020's Batman can bench press
    bench_press_2020 = bench_press_2021 - weight_diff
    #202

Topic: Power Rangers ### Response:  Question: 4 Power Rangers are in a 5-hour battle with Putty Patrollers. Each Ranger can fight for 30 minutes before they need to rest. How many times do the Rangers need to rest during the 5-hour battle?
Solution:
def solution():
    #4 Power Rangers
    rangers = 4
    #Are in a 5-hour battle
    battle_hours = 5
    #With Putty Patrollers
    patrollers = 1
    #Each Ranger can fight for 30 minutes
    fight_minutes = 30
    #Before they need to rest
    rest_minutes = 30
    #The answer is
    result = (battle_hours * 60) / (rangers * fight_minutes)
    return result

Topic: basketball ### Response:  Question: Steph Curry, the best 3-point shooter in the NBA, has made 200 3-pointers this season. He has made 50 of them in the first quarter, 40 of them in the second, 60 of them in the third, and the rest of them in the fourth. How many 3-pointers has he made in the fourth quarter?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total 3-pointers made
    total_3_pointers = 200
    #3-pointers in the first quarter
    first_quarter = 50
    #3-pointers in the second quarter
    second_quarter = 40
    #3-pointers in the third quarter
    third_quarter = 60
    #3-pointers in the fourth quarter
    fourth_quarter = total_3_pointers - first_quarter - second_quarter - third_quarter
    return fourth_quarter

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: 5000 scoops of ice cream were sold at the 2020 ice cream parade. 1000 scoops of each of the 5 flavors: vanilla, chocolate, strawberry, peanut butter, and grape were sold. How many scoops of ice cream were not sold?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total scoops of ice cream sold
    total_scoops_sold = 5000
    #Total scoops of each flavor
    scoops_per_flavor = 1000
    #Total flavors
    flavors = 5
    #Scoops sold that were not a specific flavor
    scoops_not_specific = total_scoops_sold - (scoops_per_flavor * flavors)
    return scoops_not_specific
Topic: lacrosse ### Response:  Question: A lacrosse team has 12 players. Each player is on the field for 30 minutes at a time. How many minutes does the entire team spend on the field during a 60-minute game?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Number of players
    players = 12
    #Time per player
    time_per_player = 30
    #Total game time
    total_game_time = 60
    #Total time on the field
    result = players * time_per_player
    return result

Topic: cookies ### Response:  Question: If 10 people each eat 2 cookies, how many cookies are left if there were initially 50 cookies?
Solution:
def solution():
    #10 people each eat 2 cookies
    cookies_eaten = 10 * 2
    #There were initially 50 cookies
    total_cookies = 50
    #The answer is
    result = total_cookies - cookies_eaten
    return result

    steph_age = 32
    #Steph's wife's age
    wife_age = steph_age + 2

    goalies = 2

    #Number of midfielders

Topic: Pokémon ### Response:  Question: Ash, the Pokémon trainer, has 30 Pikachu. He uses 5 of them to defeat Brock, 10 of them to defeat Misty, and 15 of them to defeat Jessie. How many Pikachu does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Ash started with 30 Pikachu
    pikachu_initial = 30
    #He used 5 of them to defeat Brock
    pikachu_used_brock = 5
    #10 of them to defeat Misty
    pikachu_used_misty = 10
    #15 of them to defeat Jessie
    pikachu_used_jessie = 15
    #The answer is
    result = pikachu_initial - pikachu_used_brock - pikachu_used_misty - pikachu_used_jessie
    return result

Topic: unicorns ### Response:  Question: 5 unicorns each ate 50 carrots. 3 unicorns each ate 40 apples. How many fruits and vegetables did the unicorns eat in all?
Solution:
def solution():
    #5 unicorns each ate 50 carrots
    unicorns = 5
    carrots_per_unicorn = 50
    carrots = unicorns * carrots_per_unicorn
    #3 unicorns each ate 40 apples
    apples_per_unicorn = 40
    apples = 3 * apples_per_unicorn
    #The total is
    total = carrots + apples
    return total

    #Blue fish

    #Green fish

    return green_fish

Topic: planes ### Response:  Question: A 747 can carry 100 people. A 777 can carry 200 people. A 787 can carry 300 people. How many people can all 3 planes carry?
Solution:
def solution():
    #747 can carry 100 people
    capacity_747 = 100
    #777 can carry 200 people
    capacity_777 = 200
    #787 can carry 300 people
    capacity_787 = 300
    #Total people all planes can carry is
    total_capacity = capacity_747 + capacity_777 + capacity_787
    return total_capacity

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response: 2022 is the year 75 million years after the Jurassic period. 50 million years after that is the year of the dinosaur extinction. How many years
ago did the dinosaurs become extinct?
Solution:
def solution():
    #2022 is 75 million years after the Jurassic period
    years_jurassic = 2022
    #50 million years after that is the year of the dinosaur extinction
    years_extinction = years_jurassic - 75
    #The dinosaurs became extinct
    result = years_extinction - 50
    return result

    peter_cookies = 21
    #Susan has 24 cookies
    susan_cookies = 24
    #If they decide to share the cookies equally between the two of them, 
    #they will each have

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response:  Question: If 1 brontosaurus weighs 4000 pounds and 1 triceratops weighs 1500 pounds, how many more pounds does a herd of 25 brontosaurus weigh than a herd of 20 triceratops? (Assume all dinosaurs are the same weight and that there is no weight difference between the two species.)
Solution:
def solution():
    #1 brontosaurus weighs 4000 pounds
    brontosaurus_weight = 4000
    #1 triceratops weighs 1500 pounds
    triceratops_weight = 1500
    #A herd of 25 brontosaurus weighs
    herd_brontosaurus_weight = brontosaurus_weight * 25
    #A herd of 20 triceratops weighs
    herd_triceratops_weight = triceratops_weight * 20
    #The answer is
    result = herd_brontosaurus_weight - herd_triceratops_weight
    return result

    total_players = 10
    #3 of the players are on the defense
    defense_players = 3
    #5 of the players are on the offense
    offense_players = 5
    #The rest are in the midfield. The answer is
    midfield_players = total_players - defense_players - offense_players
    return midfield_players

Topic: planes ### Response:  Question: A commercial airplane can hold 235 passengers. There are 4 flight attendants for every 50 passengers. How many flight attendants are on the plane?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A commercial airplane can hold 235 passengers
    passengers = 235
    #There are 4 flight attendants for every 50 passengers
    attendants_per_50_passengers = 4
    #The answer is
    result = (passengers / 50) * attendants_per_50_passengers
    return result

Topic: pizza ### Response:  Question: It cost 2 dollars for a small pizza, 4 dollars for a medium pizza, and 6 dollars for a large pizza. 

If Jimmy earned 20 dollars yesterday and 30 dollars today, how many pizzas can he buy?
Solution:
def solution():
    #It cost 2 dollars for a small pizza
    small_pizza_cost = 2
    #4 dollars for a medium pizza
    medium_pizza_cost = 4
    #6 dollars for a large pizza
    large_pizza_cost = 6
    #If Jimmy earned 20 dollars yesterday and 30 dollars today
    jimmy_earned = 20 + 30
    #Then he can buy
    small_pizzas = jimmy_earned // small_pizza_cost
    medium_pizzas = (jimmy_earned // medium_pizza_cost) % 2
    large_pizzas = jimmy_earned // large_pizza_cost
    #The answer is
    result = small_pizzas + medium_pizzas + large_pizzas
    return result

Topic: Power Rangers ### Response: 1. Question: 5 Power Rangers are in the Power Ranger command center. Blue Ranger is 15 years old, Yellow Ranger is 18 years old, Pink Ranger is 16 years old, Green Ranger is 19 years old, and Red Ranger is 18 years old. What is the average age of the Power Rangers?
Solution: def solution():
    #5 Power Rangers are in the Power Ranger command center
    num_rangers = 5
    #Blue Ranger is 15 years old
    blue_ranger_age = 15
    #Yellow Ranger is 18 years old
    yellow_ranger_age = 18
    #Pink Ranger is 16 years old
    pink_ranger_age = 16
    #Green Ranger is 19 years old
    green_ranger_age = 19
    #Red Ranger is 18 years old
    red_ranger_age = 18
    #The answer is
    result = (blue_ranger_age + yellow_ranger_age + pink_ranger_age + green_ranger_age + red_ranger_age) / num_rangers
    return result

Topic: candy ### Response:  Question: Marge has 200 candy bars. 
She is at a park with her 10 friends. 
Each of her friends takes 8 candy bars. 

How many candy bars does she have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Marge has 200 candy bars
    candy_total = 200
    #She is at a park with her 10 friends
    friends = 10
    #Each of her friends takes 8 candy bars
    candy_each = 8
    #The candy bars her friends take is
    candy_taken = friends * candy_each
    #Marge is left with
    result = candy_total - candy_taken
    return result

Topic: Minecraft ### Response:  Question: A piggy bank has 2000 Minecraft diamonds in it. 1000 of the diamonds are mined in the Nether, 500 of the diamonds are mined in the End, and the rest are mined in the Overworld. How many diamonds are mined in the Overworld?
def solution():
    #Total diamonds in the bank
    total_diamonds = 2000
    #Diamonds mined in the Nether
    nether_diamonds = 1000
    #Diamonds mined in the End
    end_diamonds = 500
    #Diamonds mined in the Overworld
    overworld_diamonds = total_diamonds - nether_diamonds - end_diamonds
    return overworld_diamonds

Topic: Super Mario ### Response:  Question: Mario has 15 coins. He gets 2 more coins from each of the 3 toads. How many coins does he have now?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Mario has 15 coins
    coins_initial = 15
    #He gets 2 more coins from each of the 3 toads
    coins_from_toads = 2 * 3
    #The answer is
    result = coins_initial + coins_from_toads
    return result

Topic: cars ### Response:  Question: 240000 cars are on a freeway. 100000 of them are in the fast lane. 60000 of them are in the slow lane. 40000 of them are in the carpool lane. How many cars are in the other lanes?
Solution:
def solution():
    #240000 cars are on a freeway
    cars_total = 240000
    #100000 of them are in the fast lane
    fast_lane = 100000
    #60000 of them are in the slow lane
    slow_lane = 60000
    #40000 of them are in the carpool lane
    carpool_lane = 40000
    #The rest of the cars are in the other lanes
    other_lanes = cars_total - fast_lane - slow_lane - carpool_lane
    #The answer is
    result = other_lanes
    return result

Topic: Iron Man ### Response:  Question: Iron Man has 5000 lasers. 3000 of them are in his chest, and the rest are in his repulsor beams. How many lasers does he have in his repulsor beams?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man has 5000 lasers
    total_lasers = 5000
    #3000 of them are in his chest
    lasers_chest = 3000
    #The rest are in his repulsor beams. The answer is
    lasers_repulsor = total_lasers - lasers_chest
    return lasers_repulsor

Topic: Barbie ### Response:  Question: Barbie has 150 outfits. She wears 20 outfits a day. How many days can she wear a different outfit every day?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Barbie has 150 outfits
    outfits = 150
    #She wears 20 outfits a day
    outfits_per_day = 20
    #The answer is
    result = outfits / outfits_per_day
    return result
Topic: Power Rangers ### Response:  Question: In the Power Rangers, each individual Power Ranger has 5 power coins. Five Power Rangers form a team, and the team has 25 power coins in total. How many power coins does each individual Power Ranger on the team have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Each individual Power Ranger has 5 power coins
    power_coins_per_ranger = 5
    #Five Power Rangers form a team
    rangers = 5
    #The team has 25 power coins in total
    total_power_coins = 25
    #The answer is
    result = total_power_coins / rangers / power_coins_per_ranger
    return result

Topic: cheer leading ### Response:  Question: 
Flint is 10 times better at cheerleading than Wanda. Wanda can do 10 cheers in 2 minutes. How many cheers can the two of them do in 4 minutes?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Wanda can do 10 cheers in 2 minutes
    wanda_per_minute = 10 / 2
    #Flint is 10 times better at cheerleading than Wanda
    flint_per_minute = 10 * wanda_per_minute
    #The answer is
    result = (wanda_per_minute + flint_per_minute) * 4
    return result

Topic: unicorns ### Response:  Question: A unicorn herd contains 20 unicorns. 50% of the unicorns are pink and 50% of the unicorns are not pink. How many unicorns are not pink?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A unicorn herd contains 20 unicorns
    total_unicorns = 20
    #50% of the unicorns are pink
    pink_unicorns = 0.50 * total_unicorns
    #50% of the unicorns are not pink
    not_pink_unicorns = 0.50 * total_unicorns
    #The answer is
    result = not_pink_unicorns
    return result

    total_trophies = 39

    grand_slam_trophies = 25
    #Sports Illustrated Swimsuit Issue Trophies
    si_swiimsuit_trophies = total_trophies - grand_slam_trophies

    #Total number of candy bars
    total_candy_bars = 200
    
    #Total number of children
    total_children = 20
    
    #Each child received the same number of candy bars. 
    
    #The answer is

    return result

Topic: Pokémon ### Response:  Question: Ash Ketchum has 50 Pokéballs. He uses 10 of them to catch Pikachu. He uses 15 of them to catch Squirtle. He uses 5 of them to catch Bulbasaur. How many Pokéballs does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Ash Ketchum has 50 Pokéballs
    pokeballs_total = 50
    #He uses 10 of them to catch Pikachu
    pokeballs_pikachu = 10
    #He uses 15 of them to catch Squirtle
    pokeballs_squirtle = 15
    #He uses 5 of them to catch Bulbasaur
    pokeballs_bulbasaur = 5
    #The answer is
    pokeballs_left = pokeballs_total - pokeballs_pikachu - pokeballs_squirtle - pokeballs_bulbasaur
    return pokeballs_left

Topic: volleyball ### Response:  Question: 12 volleyball players are lined up in 2 rows of 6. 2 of the players are assigned to the libero position. How many players are left in the court?
Solution:
def solution():
    #12 volleyball players are lined up in 2 rows of 6
    players_initial = 12
    #2 of the players are assigned to the libero position
    liberos = 2
    #The answer is
    result = players_initial - liberos
    return result

The flight from Philadelphia to Los Angeles takes 5 hours and the flight from Boston to Los Angeles takes 7 hours. He can choose to fly from either airport. If he flies from Philadelphia, he will have to take a 2-hour train ride from New York to Philadelphia. If he flies from Boston, he will have to take a 3-hour train ride from New York to Boston. How much longer is the total trip from New York to Los Angeles if Mario flies from Philadelphia instead of Boston?
Solution:
def solution():

    # Flight times (in hours)
    flight_PA_to_LA = 5
    flight_Boston_to_LA = 7

    # Train times (in hours)
    train_PA = 2
    train_Boston = 3

    # Total trip times from New York to Los Angeles if Mario flies from Philadelphia
    total_trip_PA = flight_PA_to_LA + train_PA

    # Total trip times from New York to Los Angeles if Mario flies from Boston
    total_trip_Boston = flight_Boston_to_LA + train_Boston

    # Difference in total

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: 30000 scoops of ice cream were sold. Each scoop of ice cream has 250 calories. How many calories were sold?
Solution:
def solution():
    #30000 scoops of ice cream were sold
    scoops_sold = 30000
    #Each scoop of ice cream has 250 calories
    calories_per_scoop = 250
    #The answer is
    result = scoops_sold * calories_per_scoop
    return result
Topic: Thor, the God of Thunder ### Response: 24 lightning bolts were forged by the Dwarves. Thor, the God of Thunder, has 4000. He hurls 500 of them at the Frost Giants. He then hurls 2000 of them at the Rock Giants. How many lightning bolts does he have left?

import math

#Initial number of lightning bolts
initial = 4000

#Number of lightning bolts forged by the Dwarves
dwarves = 24

#Number of lightning bolts hurls at the Frost Giants
frost = 500

#Number of lightning bolts hurls at the Rock Giants
rock = 2000

#Number of lightning bolts remaining

Topic: Power Rangers ### Response:  Question: 5 Power Rangers are in a fight with 15 Putties. 2 of the Putties are pink. 3 of the Putties are green. 5 of the Putties are blue. 5 of the Putties are yellow. 5 of the Putties are red. How many Putties are left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #5 Power Rangers are in a fight with 15 Putties
    putties_initial = 15
    #2 of the Putties are pink
    putties_pink = 2
    #3 of the Putties are green
    putties_green = 3
    #5 of the Putties are blue
    putties_blue = 5
    #5 of the Putties are yellow
    putties_yellow = 5
    #5 of the Putties are red
    putties_red = 5
    #The answer is
    result = putties_initial - putties_pink - putties_green - putties_blue - putties_yellow - putties_red
    return result
Topic: Taylor Swift ### Response:  Question: Taylor Swift is the wealthiest celebrity. She has 1000 cars. She has 100 more yachts than boats. She has 10 times as many boats as private planes. How many private planes does Taylor Swift have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of cars Taylor Swift has
    cars = 1000
    #She has 100 more yachts than boats
    yachts = cars + 100
    #She has 10 times as many boats as private planes
    private_planes = yachts / 10
    return private_planes

Topic: Taylor Swift ### Response:  Question: Taylor Swift has 2000 fans. 500 of them are in the front row, 500 are in the 2nd row, and 500 are in the 3rd row. 500 more fans are in the 4th row. How many fans are in the 5th row?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Taylor Swift has 2000 fans
    fans_total = 2000
    #500 of them are in the front row
    fans_front_row = 500
    #500 are in the 2nd row
    fans_2nd_row = 500
    #500 are in the 3rd row
    fans_3rd_row = 500
    #500 more fans are in the 4th row
    fans_4th_row = 500
    #The fans in the 5th row are the total fans minus the fans in the front, 2nd, 3rd, and 4th rows
    fans_5th_row = fans_total - fans_front_row - fans_2nd_row - fans_3rd_row - fans_4th_row
    #The answer is
    result = fans_5

Topic: Ninja Turtles ### Response:  Question: There are 4 Ninja Turtles. 2 of them, Raphael and Michelangelo, are 21 years old. The others, Donatello and Leonardo, are 18 years old. What is the average age of the 4 Ninja Turtles?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The number of Ninja Turtles
    turtles = 4
    #The number of turtles that are 21 years old
    turtles_21 = 2
    #The number of turtles that are 18 years old
    turtles_18 = turtles - turtles_21
    #The average age is
    result = (turtles_21 * 21 + turtles_18 * 18) / turtles
    return result
Topic: cars ### Response:  Question: A parking garage can hold 100 cars in 3 stories. 20% of the spots on each floor are for motorcycles. How many total spots are there for cars and motorcycles?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A parking garage can hold 100 cars in 3 stories
    cars_per_story = 100 / 3
    #20% of the spots on each floor are for motorcycles
    motorcycles_per_story = cars_per_story * 0.2
    #There are 3 stories
    total_motorcycles = motorcycles_per_story * 3
    #The spots for cars are
    cars_total = cars_per_story * 3
    #The total spots are
    total_spots = cars_total + total_motorcycles
    return total_spots

Topic: Spiderman ### Response:  Question: Spiderman can web-sling 1500 feet in the air. He can web-sling 500 feet vertically and 1000 feet horizontally. How high and how far can he web-sling in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Spiderman can web-sling 1500 feet in the air
    total_feet_3d = 1500
    #He can web-sling 500 feet vertically and 1000 feet horizontally
    feet_vertical = 500
    feet_horizontal = 1000
    #The answer is
    result = [total_feet_3d, feet_vertical + feet_horizontal]
    return result

Topic: candy ### Response:  Question: 5000 candies were in a candy bowl. 1000 candies were taken out of the candy bowl. 250 candies were added to the candy bowl. How many candies are in the candy bowl now?
Solution:

    #5000 candies were in a candy bowl
    candies_initial = 5000
    #1000 candies were taken out of the candy bowl
    candies_taken = 1000
    #250 candies were added to the candy bowl
    candies_added = 250
    #The answer is
    result = candies_initial - candies_taken + candies_added
    return result

Topic: Wonder Woman ### Response:  Question: Wonder Woman can lasso 500 people. 200 of the people she lassos are evil. 100 of the evil people are the league of injustice. How many of the people she lassos are not evil or in the league of injustice?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Wonder Woman can lasso 500 people
    total_people = 500
    #200 of the people she lassos are evil
    evil_people = 200
    #100 of the evil people are the league of injustice
    league_injustice = 100
    #The people who are not evil or in the league of injustice are
    non_evil_non_league = total_people - evil_people - league_injustice
    #The answer is
    result = non_evil_non_league
    return result

Topic: Thor, the God of Thunder ### Response:  Question: 8000 people were at a Thor convention. 500 of them left in the first hour. 200 more left in the second hour. 300 more left in the third hour. How many people were left at the rally at the end of the third hour?
Solution:
def solution():
    #There were 8000 people at the rally
    people_initial = 8000
    #500 left in the first hour
    people_left_first_hour = 500
    #200 more left in the second hour
    people_left_second_hour = 200
    #300 more left in the third hour
    people_left_third_hour = 300
    #The answer is
    result = people_initial - people_left_first_hour - people_left_second_hour - people_left_third_hour
    return result
Topic: football ### Response:  Question: In a 2023 Super Bowl, for a particular play, the Kansas City Chiefs had an offense of 412 square inches and the Philadelphia Eagles had an offense of 472 square inches. How many more square inches did the Philadelphia Eagles have than the Kansas City Chiefs?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The offense of Kansas City Chiefs
    kansas_city_offense = 412
    #The offense of Philadelphia Eagles
    philadelphia_eagles_offense = 472
    #The answer is
    result = philadelphia_eagles_offense - kansas_city_offense
    return result
Topic: football ### Response:  Question: Tom has 3 friends. 2 of them play American football, and the other one plays soccer. If Tom plays American football, how many people will be on his team if each friend brings 3 more friends?
Solution:

    #Tom has 3 friends
    friends_tom = 3
    #2 of them play American football
    american_football_friends = 2
    #The other one plays soccer
    soccer_friend = 1
    #If Tom plays American football, how many people will be on his team if each friend brings 3 more friends?
    friends_bring_more = 3
    #The answer is
    result = friends_tom + american_football_friends + friends_bring_more
    return result

Topic: planes ### Response:  Question: A pilot is flying a plane that weighs 1000 pounds. He needs to fly the plane for 500 miles. Each mile the plane flies costs 10 pounds of fuel. How much fuel does the plane need?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The plane weighs 1000 pounds
    plane_weight = 1000
    #He needs to fly it for 500 miles
    miles = 500
    #Each mile it flies costs 10 pounds of fuel
    fuel_per_mile = 10
    #The answer is
    result = plane_weight + miles * fuel_per_mile
    return result

Topic: candy ### Response:  Question: Barry has 20 lollipops, 40 M&Ms, and 60 Swizzles.  If he eats 10 lollipops, 20 M&Ms, and 30 Swizzles, how many candies does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Barry initially has
    lollipops_initial = 20
    mms_initial = 40
    swizzles_initial = 60
    #Barry eats
    lollipops_eaten = 10
    mms_eaten = 20
    swizzles_eaten = 30
    #Barry is left with
    lollipops_left = lollipops_initial - lollipops_eaten
    mms_left = mms_initial - mms_eaten
    swizzles_left = swizzles_initial - swizzles_eaten
    #Total candies left
    total_candies_left = lollipops_left + mms_left + swizzles_left
    return total_candies_left

Topic: cheer leading ### Response:  Question: A group of 24 cheerleaders is leading a 5-kilometer race. They start the race with 8 pom-poms each. 

1. The first 3 kilometers of the race, the cheerleaders are so excited that they drop 10 pom-poms each. 

2. The next 2 kilometers, the cheerleaders are so tired that they drop 5 pom-poms each. 

3. The final kilometers, the cheerleaders are so exhausted that they only have 4 pom-poms each. 

How many pom-poms are left in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total cheerleaders
    total_cheerleaders = 24
    #Pom-poms each cheerleader has initially
    initial_pom_poms = 8
    #Total pom-poms initially
    total_initial_pom_poms = total_cheerleaders * initial_pom_poms
    #Lost pom-poms in the first 3 kilometers
    lost_pom_poms_1 = 10
    #Total pom-poms lost in the first 3 kilometers
    total_lost_pom_poms_1 = total_cheerleaders * lost_pom_poms_1

Topic: cheer leading ### Response: 1000 Hello Kitty toys are to be shipped to the warehouse. 200 of them are pink, 300 of them are blue, and the rest are white. How many of the toys are white?
Solution:

    #Total toys
    total_toys = 1000
    #Pink toys
    pink_toys = 200
    #Blue toys
    blue_toys = 300
    #White toys are the rest
    white_toys = total_toys - pink_toys - blue_toys

Solution:

    #Black Panther has 52 vibranium bullets
    bullets_initial = 52
    #He fires 10 at each of the 3 Hulk monsters
    bullets_fired = 10 * 3
    #He has
    bullets_left = bullets_initial - bullets_fired
    return bullets_left
Topic: football ### Response:  Question: Tom has 12 footballs. 20% of them are red, 40% are green, and the rest are blue. How many are blue?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Tom has 12 footballs
    total_footballs = 12
    #20% of them are red
    red_percent = 0.2
    #40% are green
    green_percent = 0.4
    #The rest are blue
    blue_percent = 1 - red_percent - green_percent
    #The answer is
    blue_footballs = total_footballs * blue_percent
    return blue_footballs

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response:  Question: Captain Marvel has 5000 photon blasts. She used 2000 on the Kree and 1500 on the Skrulls. How many photon blasts does she have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain Marvel started with 5000 photon blasts
    photon_blasts_start = 5000
    #She used 2000 on the Kree
    photon_blasts_used_kree = 2000
    #and 1500 on the Skrulls
    photon_blasts_used_skrulls = 1500
    #The answer is
    result = photon_blasts_start - photon_blasts_used_kree - photon_blasts_used_skrulls
    return result

Topic: trains ### Response:  Question: 15 trains left the train station. Each train has 4 carriages. If 20 people got on each train, how many people are on the trains?
Solution:
def solution():
    #15 trains left the station
    trains = 15
    #Each train has 4 carriages
    carriages_per_train = 4
    #20 people got on each train
    people_per_train = 20
    #15 trains with 4 carriages each equals
    total_carriages = trains * carriages_per_train
    #20 people on each of these 15 trains is
    total_people = total_carriages * people_per_train
    #The answer is
    result = total_people
    return result

Topic: Minecraft ### Response:  Question: A Minecraft world has 1000 blocks. 

Alice mined 200 blocks of coal, 

Bob mined 500 blocks of dirt, 

Charlie mined 200 blocks of iron, 

David mined 300 blocks of redstone, and 

Eve mined 200 blocks of stone.

How many blocks do the four players have in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A Minecraft world has 1000 blocks
    blocks_total = 1000
    #Alice mined 200 blocks of coal
    blocks_alice = 200
    #Bob mined 500 blocks of dirt
    blocks_bob = 500
    #Charlie mined 200 blocks of iron
    blocks_charlie = 200
    #David mined 300 blocks of redstone
    blocks_david = 300
    #Eve mined 200 blocks of stone
    blocks_eve = 200
    #The answer is
    result = blocks_alice + blocks_bob + blocks_charlie + blocks_david + blocks_eve
    return result

Topic: planes ### Response:  Question: A plane is 2000 feet long. A runway is 10 times that long. How many planes can land on the runway?
Solution:
def solution():
    # length of a plane in feet
    plane_length = 2000
    # length of the runway in feet
    runway_length = 10 * plane_length
    # number of planes that can land on the runway
    num_planes = runway_length // plane_length
    return num_planes

Topic: soccer ### Response:  Question: 200 soccer players are in a stadium. 100 of them are boys and 100 of them are girls. 50 of the boys are on the soccer team. 20 of the girls are on the soccer team.  How many soccer players are not on the soccer team?
Solution:
def solution():
    #200 soccer players are in a stadium
    total_players = 200
    #100 of them are boys and 100 of them are girls
    boys = 100
    girls = 100
    #50 of the boys are on the soccer team
    boys_on_team = 50
    #20 of the girls are on the soccer team
    girls_on_team = 20
    #The answer is
    result = total_players - (boys_on_team + girls_on_team)
    return result

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response:  Question: A 5000-year-old alien spaceship is traveling at 1000 miles per second. How many miles does it travel in 5 years?

Solution:

def solution():

    # convert years to seconds, using 3.154*10^7 seconds per year
    years_to_seconds = 5 * 3.154 * 10**7

    # distance traveled in 1 second
    distance_per_second = 1000

    # total distance traveled in 5 years
    total_distance = years_to_seconds * distance_per_second

    return total_distance

    total_dora_milaje = 12
    #Dora Milaje in the movie
    dora_milaje_movie = 6
    #Dora Milaje in the comics
    dora_milaje_comics = total_dora_milaje - dora_milaje_movie
    return dora_milaje_comics

    return solution()

    print(solve())
This solution calculates the number of Dora Milaje in the comics. 12 Dora Milaje total, 6 in the movie, so the rest (12 - 6) must be in the comics.
Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: 8 scoops of ice cream weigh 32 ounces. 
Alice, Bob, and Charlie are each trying to eat 3 scoops of ice cream. 
How many ounces of ice cream are they eating?
Solution:
def solution():
    #8 scoops of ice cream weigh 32 ounces
    scoops_per_ounce = 8 / 32
    #Alice, Bob, and Charlie are each trying to eat 3 scoops of ice cream
    scoops_per_person = 3
    #There are 3 of them
    people = 3
    #The answer is
    result = scoops_per_ounce * scoops_per_person * people
    return result

Topic: Power Rangers ### Response:  Question: 5 Power Rangers are in a 15-episode series. 3 of them are in every episode. 2 of them are in 10 episodes. How many episodes does the 5th Power Ranger appear in?

Solution:
def solution():
    #5 Power Rangers are in a 15-episode series
    total_episodes = 15
    #3 of them are in every episode
    rangers_in_every_episode = 3
    #2 of them are in 10 episodes
    rangers_in_10_episodes = 2
    #The 5th Power Ranger is in
    rangers_in_10_episodes * 10
    fiveth_ranger_episodes = 0
    #The answer is
    result = total_episodes - (rangers_in_every_episode * 3) - (rangers_in_10_episodes * 10) - fiveth_ranger_episodes
    return result

How much power do the Power Rangers in the city have?

    power_total = 1000
    #5 of the Power Rangers are in the city
    power_rangers_city = 5

Topic: lacrosse ### Response:  Question: 

Jacob is 10 years old and plays on a lacrosse team with 20 other boys. 

He is the only one on the team who is 10 years old. 

How many years older, on average, are the other boys on the team than Jacob?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Jacob is 10 years old
    jacob_age = 10
    #He is the only 10-year-old on the team
    other_boys_age = 20
    #The average age of the other boys is
    average_age = (other_boys_age - jacob_age) / (other_boys_age - 1)
    return average_age

Topic: planes ### Response:  Question: There were 300 passengers on a plane. 2/3 of the passengers were adults. 50 of the adults were in first class. 60 of the adults were in business class. The rest of the adults were in economy class. How many adults were in economy class?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of passengers
    total_passengers = 300
    #Number of adults
    adults = total_passengers * 2 / 3
    #Number of adults in first class
    first_class = 50
    #Number of adults in business class
    business_class = 60
    #Number of adults in economy class
    economy_class = adults - first_class - business_class
    #The answer is
    result = economy_class
    return result

Topic: dogs ### Response:  Question: Mike has 3 German Shepherds, 4 Golden Retrievers, and 5 French Bulldogs. If each German Shepherd weighs 80 pounds, each Golden Retriever weighs 75 pounds, and each French Bulldog weighs 28 pounds, what is the average weight of all of Mike's dogs?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Mike has 3 German Shepherds, 4 Golden Retrievers, and 5 French Bulldogs.
    german_shepherd_count = 3
    golden_retriever_count = 4
    french_bulldog_count = 5
    #Each German Shepherd weighs 80 pounds.
    german_shepherd_weight = 80
    #Each Golden Retriever weighs 75 pounds.
    golden_retriever_weight = 75
    #Each French Bulldog weighs 28 pounds.
    french_bulldog_weight = 28
    #The average weight of all of Mike's dogs is
    total_weight = (german_shepherd_count * german_shepherd_weight) + (golden_retriever_count * golden_retriever_weight) + (french_bulldog_count * french_bulldog_weight)

Topic: lacrosse ### Response:  Question: A lacrosse team has 12 players. 1/3 of the players are left-handed. 1/4 of the left-handed players switch to right-handed. 1/6 of the right-handed players then switch to two-handed. How many players are there now?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of players
    total_players = 12
    #Number of left-handed players
    left_handed = total_players / 3
    #Number of left-handed players who switch to right-handed
    left_handed_switch = left_handed / 4
    #Number of right-handed players who switch to two-handed
    right_handed_switch = (total_players - left_handed) / 6
    #The answer is the total number of players after the switches
    result = total_players - left_handed_switch + right_handed_switch
    return result
#In this task, the students are solving a word problem that involves a series of switches between different playing styles in the sport of lacrosse. 1/3 of the players are left-handed, 1/4 of those switch to right-handed, and 1/6 of the right-handed players switch to
Topic: basketball ### Response: 1. A basketball team has 5 players. 2. Each player scores 3 points per game. 3. The team plays 20 games. What is the total number of points the team scores?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A basketball team has 5 players
    players = 5
    #Each player scores 3 points per game
    points_per_game = 3
    #The team plays 20 games
    games = 20
    #The total number of points the team scores is
    result = players * points_per_game * games
    return result

def solution():
    #A 3-gallon tub of ice cream has 150 scoops
    scoops_total = 150
    #6 people each have 2 scoops
    people_2scoops = 6 * 2
    #3 people have 3 scoops
    people_3scoops = 3 * 3
    #The remaining scoops are
    scoops_remaining = scoops_total - people_2scoops - people_3scoops
    return scoops_remaining

    #Peter pays $20 for 10 lollipops
    lollipops_cost = 20
    #Each lollipop contains 5 sticks of candy
    sticks_per_lollipop = 5
    #Total sticks of candy
    total_sticks = lollipops_cost / 10 * sticks_per_lollipop
    #The cost of each stick of candy
    cost_per_stick = lollipops_cost / total_sticks
    #Convert the cost to cents
    result = cost_per_stick * 100
    return result

Topic: cookies ### Response:  Question: Michael and Emily are baking cookies. Michael bakes 10 cookies every 20 minutes. Emily bakes 5 cookies every 20 minutes. They bake for 60 minutes. How many cookies do they bake in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Michael bakes 10 cookies every 20 minutes
    michael_bakes_per_minute = 10 / 20
    #Emily bakes 5 cookies every 20 minutes
    emily_bakes_per_minute = 5 / 20
    #They bake for 60 minutes
    time_baking = 60
    #The total number of cookies they bake is
    total_cookies = (michael_bakes_per_minute + emily_bakes_per_minute) * time_baking
    return total_cookies
Topic: lacrosse ### Response:  Question: 20 players on each team are on the field. 80% of the players on each team are boys. 10% of the boys on each team are captains. How many captains are on the field?
Solution:
def solution():
    #20 players on each team are on the field
    players_per_team = 20
    #80% of the players on each team are boys
    boys_per_team = 0.8 * players_per_team
    #10% of the boys on each team are captains
    captains_per_team = 0.1 * boys_per_team
    #The answer is
    result = 2 * captains_per_team
    return result

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Problem: 
3 scoops of ice cream cost $5. 
How much does 20 scoops of ice cream cost?
Solution:

    cost_3_scoops = 5
    #cost per scoop
    cost_per_scoop = cost_3_scoops / 3
    #cost of 20 scoops
    cost_20_scoops = cost_per_scoop * 20
    return cost_20_scoops
Topic: pizza ### Response:  Question: 4 friends are ordering pizza. Each person wants 3 slices. The pizza is 18 slices. How many more slices does the pizza need to be to have enough for everyone?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Number of friends
    friends = 4
    #Slices each friend wants
    slices_per_friend = 3
    #Total slices needed
    total_slices_needed = friends * slices_per_friend
    #Pizza is 18 slices
    pizza_slices = 18
    #More slices needed
    more_slices_needed = total_slices_needed - pizza_slices
    return more_slices_needed

Topic: basketball ### Response:  Question: Steph Curry, the best 3-point shooter of all time, is on a 3-point shooting tear. He starts a game with 0 points and makes 3-pointers at the rate of 1 every 2 points. After he has scored 50 points, how many 3-pointers has he made?

    points_per_3pointer = 2
    #He scored 50 points during the game

Topic: volleyball ### Response: 12 volleyball players on a team. 2 teams play 3 sets each. 1 player from each team is substituted in each set. How many players are on the court at the same time?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Players per team
    players_per_team = 12
    #Teams
    teams = 2
    #Sets
    sets = 3
    #Substitutions per set
    substitutions_per_set = 1
    #Total players on the court
    total_players = players_per_team * teams * sets - substitutions_per_set * sets
    return total_players

Topic: pizza ### Response:  Question: How many slices of pizza do you get if you buy 3 large pizzas that have 16 slices each and you give 4 slices to your friends?
Solution:
def solution():
    #3 large pizzas with 16 slices each
    slices_total = 3 * 16
    #Slices given to friends
    slices_friends = 4
    #Slices left
    slices_left = slices_total - slices_friends
    return slices_left

    #I eat 3 candies a day
    candies_per_day = 3

Topic: football ### Response:  Question: On Tuesday, 12 football players weighed in. 

20 of them weighed more than 120kg. 

30 of them weighed less than 110kg. 

The rest weighed between 110kg and 120kg. How many players did weigh between 110kg and 120kg?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total players
    total_players = 12
    #Players who weigh more than 120kg
    more = 20
    #Players who weigh less than 110kg
    less = 30
    #Players who weigh between 110kg and 120kg
    between = total_players - more - less
    return between
Topic: cats ### Response:  Question: Mr. Peterson has 100 cats. 60 of them are Siamese, 20 of them are Persians, and the rest are Maine Coon cats. How many Maine Coon cats does he have?

    #Mr. Peterson has 100 cats
    total_cats = 100
    #60 of them are Siamese
    siamese_cats = 60
    #20 of them are Persians
    persian_cats = 20
    #The rest are Maine Coon cats
    maine_coon_cats = total_cats - siamese_cats - persian_cats
    #The answer is
    result = maine_coon_cats
    return result

    #3-person squad
    squad = 3
    #Each cheerleader has 2 pom poms
    pom_poms_per_cheerleader = 2
    #1 of the cheerleaders is a captain and gets 1 more pom pom
    captain_pom_poms = 1
    #The total number of pom poms is

    return result

Topic: Superman ### Response:  Question:  Superman is 1000 times stronger than a normal human.  He is 2000 times faster than a normal human.  He is 5000 times more powerful than a normal human.  How many times more impressive is he than 3 normal humans?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman is 1000 times stronger than a normal human
    strength_ratio = 1000
    #He is 2000 times faster than a normal human
    speed_ratio = 2000
    #He is 5000 times more powerful than a normal human
    power_ratio = 5000
    #3 normal humans is
    normal_humans = 3
    #The answer is
    result = (strength_ratio * speed_ratio * power_ratio) / normal_humans
    return result

    #He made 20 shots
    shots_total = 20
    #10 of them were from the field and 5 of them were from the 3-point line

Topic: Super Mario ### Response:  Question: In a 10-level Mario game, it took 100 minutes to finish the first 5 levels. The next 3 levels took twice as long. It then took another 100 minutes to finish the last 2 levels. How long did it take to finish the whole game?  Python code:
def solution():
    #It took 100 minutes to finish the first 5 levels
    first_5_levels = 100
    #The next 3 levels took twice as long
    next_3_levels = 2 * first_5_levels
    #It then took another 100 minutes to finish the last 2 levels
    last_2_levels = 100
    #The total time is
    result = first_5_levels + next_3_levels + last_2_levels
    return result

Topic: Steph Curry ### Response: 3-Point Shots:

Steph Curry is a professional basketball player. He is known for his 3-point shooting. In 2021, he made 251 3-point shots. 40% of these were in the 4th quarter. How many 3-point shots did he make in the 4th quarter?
Solution:
def solution():
    #He made 251 3-point shots in 2021
    total_3_point_shots = 251
    #40% of these were in the 4th quarter
    fourth_quarter_percent = 40
    #The answer is
    result = (total_3_point_shots * fourth_quarter_percent) / 100
    return result

Topic: basketball ### Response:  Question: 

A basketball team has 12 players. 

- 5 of the players are 12 years old 
- 3 of the players are 13 years old 
- 2 of the players are 14 years old 
- 2 of the players are 15 years old

What is the average age of the players on the basketball team?

Solution:

def solution():
    #Total players
    total_players = 12
    #Players of each age
    players_12 = 5
    players_13 = 3
    players_14 = 2
    players_15 = 2
    #Total players of each age
    total_players_12 = players_12
    total_players_13 = players_13
    total_players_14 = players_14
    total_players_15 = players_15
    #The total players of all ages is
    total_total_players = total_players
    #The average age is
    result = (players_12 * 12 + players_13 * 13 + players_14 * 14 + players_15 * 15) / total_total_players
    return result

Topic: field hockey ### Response: 12 field hockey players in 3 teams. Each team has 4 players. How many more players are needed for 5 teams?
Solution:
def solution():
    #12 players in 3 teams
    players = 12
    #Each team has 4 players
    team_size = 4
    #Number of teams needed for 5 teams
    total_teams = 5
    #Number of players needed for 5 teams
    players_needed = total_teams * team_size
    #The answer is
    result = players_needed - players
    return result

Topic: soccer ### Response:  Question: There were 3000 people at a soccer game. 2500 of them were in the stands and the rest were on the field. 1500 of the people on the field were soccer players and the rest were referees and officials. How many referees and officials were at the game?
Solution:
def solution():
    #There were 3000 people at the soccer game
    total_people = 3000
    #2500 of them were in the stands
    people_in_stands = 2500
    #The rest were on the field
    people_on_field = total_people - people_in_stands
    #1500 of the people on the field were soccer players
    soccer_players = 1500
    #The rest were referees and officials. The answer is
    referees_and_officials = people_on_field - soccer_players
    return referees_and_officials
Topic: Harry Potter ### Response:  Question: 

Professor Dumbledore assigned 150 pages of reading over the weekend. 

Ron, who does not like to read, only managed to read 30 pages. 

Neville, who is very slow, took all weekend to read just 10 pages. 

Harry, being the good student that he is, read 2/3 of the assignment. 

How many more pages did Harry read than Ron and Neville combined?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The total number of pages assigned
    total_pages = 150
    #Ron's pages
    ron_pages = 30
    #Neville's pages
    neville_pages = 10
    #Harry's pages
    harry_pages = total_pages * 2 / 3
    #The answer is
    result = harry_pages - ron_pages - neville_pages
    return result

Topic: Power Rangers ### Response:  Question: The Power Rangers are in a fight with the Putties. 

Each Power Ranger has 5 punches. 

Each Putty has 20 punches. 

How many punches do the Power Rangers have in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Each Power Ranger has 5 punches
    punches_per_ranger = 5
    #Each Putty has 20 punches
    punches_per_putty = 20
    #There are 5 Putties
    putties = 5
    #The answer is
    result = punches_per_ranger * 5 - punches_per_putty * putties
    return result

    return result

Topic: Captain America ### Response:  Question:  There were 1000 Nazis at the concentration camp. 500 of them were sent to the gas chambers. 200 of them were hanged. 300 of them were set free. How many Nazis are left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #There were 1000 Nazis at the concentration camp
    nazis_initial = 1000
    #500 of them were sent to the gas chambers
    nazis_gas_chambers = 500
    #200 of them were hanged
    nazis_hanged = 200
    #300 of them were set free
    nazis_set_free = 300
    #The answer is
    result = nazis_initial - nazis_gas_chambers - nazis_hanged + nazis_set_free
    return result

    miles_per_hour = 1000
    #He flies for 10 hours a day for 7 days

    #The answer is

Topic: Super Mario ### Response:  Question: Super Mario is a plumber. He has to fix 100 pipes. Each pipe takes 10 minutes to fix. How many hours will it take him to fix all the pipes?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Super Mario has to fix 100 pipes
    pipes = 100
    #Each pipe takes 10 minutes to fix
    minutes_per_pipe = 10
    #The total time is
    total_minutes = pipes * minutes_per_pipe
    #That is
    hours = total_minutes / 60
    #The answer is
    result = hours
    return result

Topic: football ### Response:  Question: Tom has 15 football players on his team. 8 of them are on the offense, 4 of them are on the defense, and the rest are on special teams. How many players are on special teams?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total players
    total_players = 15
    #Offense
    offense = 8
    #Defense
    defense = 4
    #Special teams
    special_teams = total_players - offense - defense
    return special_teams
Given the function $f(x) = x^2 - 2x - 8$, find the values of $x$ that satisfy the equation $f(x) = 4$.

## Python Program to find the Solutions
import sympy as sp

# Define the function
x = sp.symbols('x')
f = x**2 - 2*x - 8

# Define the equation
equation = f - 4

# Solve the equation
solution = sp.solve(equation, x)

# Print the solutions
print(solution)

Topic: Thor, the God of Thunder ### Response:  Question: Thor has 15 hammers. He threw 5 hammers at Loki. Loki dropped 3 hammers. How many hammers does Thor have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Thor started with 15 hammers
    hammers_initial = 15
    #He threw 5 at Loki
    hammers_thrown = 5
    #Loki dropped 3 hammers
    hammers_dropped = 3
    #The answer is
    result = hammers_initial - hammers_thrown + hammers_dropped
    return result

Topic: dogs ### Response:  Question: 20 of the dogs in the park are Dachshunds. 40% of the Dachshunds are wearing doggie bandanas. 20% of the Dachshunds wearing doggie bandanas are also wearing a doggie onesie. How many Dachshunds are wearing both a doggie bandana and a doggie onesie?
Solution:
def solution():
    #20 of the dogs in the park are Dachshunds
    dachshunds = 20
    #40% of the Dachshunds are wearing doggie bandanas
    bandanas = 0.40 * dachshunds
    #20% of the Dachshunds wearing doggie bandanas are also wearing a doggie onesie
    onesies = 0.20 * bandanas
    #The answer is
    result = int(onesies)
    return result

Topic: cats ### Response:  Question: 120 cats are in a cat park. 40% of the cats are orange. 20% of the cats are grey. 30% of the cats are white. How many cats are not any of these colors?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of cats
    total_cats = 120
    #Percentage of orange cats
    orange_percentage = 40
    #Percentage of grey cats
    grey_percentage = 20
    #Percentage of white cats
    white_percentage = 30
    #The answer is
    orange_cats = total_cats * (orange_percentage / 100)
    grey_cats = total_cats * (grey_percentage / 100)
    white_cats = total_cats * (white_percentage / 100)
    cats_not_colored = total_cats - orange_cats - grey_cats - white_cats
    return cats_not_colored

    return toyotas_equal_to_fords

Topic: Hello Kitty ### Response:  Question: Hello Kitty has 12 apples. She eats 3 of them, and the rest are divided into 3 equally-sized piles. How many apples are in each pile?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Hello Kitty has 12 apples
    apples_initial = 12
    #She eats 3 of them
    apples_eaten = 3
    #The rest are divided into 3 equally-sized piles
    piles = 3
    #The answer is
    result = (apples_initial - apples_eaten) / piles
    return result
Topic: Taylor Swift ### Response: 12th-grade math is tough, but 24-7 Taylor Swift education is even tougher. Taylor Swift has 12 albums, and each album has 15 songs. Taylor Swift is releasing a new album every month. How many songs does Taylor Swift have to study in 12th grade?

    albums = 12
    songs_per_album = 15

    months_in_12th_grade = 12
    #The number of songs she has to study is

Topic: Batman ### Response:  Question:  Batman is a superhero who is a billionaire.  He buys 20 toys for each of the 10 orphanages in Gotham.  He then buys 50 toys for each of the 10 children's hospitals in Gotham.  How many toys does he buy in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Number of orphanages
    orphanages = 10
    #Number of toys for each orphanage
    toys_per_orphanage = 20
    #Total toys for orphanages
    toys_orphanages = orphanages * toys_per_orphanage
    #Number of children's hospitals
    hospitals = 10
    #Number of toys for each hospital
    toys_per_hospital = 50
    #Total toys for hospitals
    toys_hospitals = hospitals * toys_per_hospital
    #Total toys bought
    total_toys = toys_orphanages + toys_hospitals
    return total_toys

Topic: Iron Man ### Response:  Question: Iron Man is a superhero who flies with a jetpack. He has 12 charges for his jetpack. He flies for 3 minutes on each charge. How far does he fly in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man has 12 charges for his jetpack
    charges = 12
    #He flies for 3 minutes on each charge
    minutes_per_charge = 3
    #The total time he flies is
    total_minutes = charges * minutes_per_charge
    #The answer is
    result = total_minutes * 60  # converting minutes to kilometers as 1 minute = 1.6 kilometers
    return result

Topic: cats ### Response:  Question: There are 4000 cats in a city. 2500 of them are in the north part of the city. 1500 of them are in the south part of the city. How many cats are in the center of the city?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of cats in the city
    total_cats = 4000
    #Number of cats in the north part of the city
    north_cats = 2500
    #Number of cats in the south part of the city
    south_cats = 1500
    #The number of cats in the center of the city is
    center_cats = total_cats - north_cats - south_cats
    return center_cats

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: If one scoop of ice cream is 100 calories, and each person in our family needs 2 scoops of ice cream, how many scoops of ice cream do we need for the entire family of 4?
Solution:
def solution():
    #One scoop of ice cream is 100 calories
    calories_per_scoop = 100
    #Each person in our family needs 2 scoops of ice cream
    scoops_per_person = 2
    #There are 4 people in our family
    family_size = 4
    #The total number of scoops needed is
    result = calories_per_scoop * scoops_per_person * family_size
    return result

    #Number of players sent off the field
    players_sent_off = yellow_cards / 2
    #Number of

Topic: trains ### Response:  Question: 10 cargo trains can carry 100000 pounds of cargo. 5 of the trains are 1000 feet long. 2 of the trains are 2000 feet long. 3 of the trains are 5000 feet long. How many pounds of cargo can the trains carry?
Solution:
def solution():
    #10 cargo trains can carry 100000 pounds of cargo
    trains = 10
    cargo_per_train = 100000
    #5 of the trains are 1000 feet long
    short_trains = 5
    #2 of the trains are 2000 feet long
    medium_trains = 2
    #3 of the trains are 5000 feet long
    long_trains = 3
    #The answer is
    result = (short_trains + medium_trains + long_trains) * cargo_per_train
    return result

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: If there are 50 scoops of ice cream in a tub, and 10 people eat 4 scoops each, how much ice cream is left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #There are 50 scoops of ice cream in a tub
    total_scoops = 50
    #10 people eat 4 scoops each
    people = 10
    scoops_per_person = 4
    #They ate
    scoops_consumed = people * scoops_per_person
    #The answer is
    result = total_scoops - scoops_consumed
    return result

    trophies_living_room = 100
    #50 of the trophies are in her garage

Topic: Superman ### Response:  Question: Superman can fly at a speed of 2000 miles per hour. He flies from Metropolis to Gotham City, which is 1000 miles away. He then flies to the Fortress of Solitude, which is 2000 miles away from Gotham City. How many hours does it take Superman to travel from Metropolis to the Fortress of Solitude?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman can fly at a speed of 2000 miles per hour
    superman_speed = 2000
    #He flies from Metropolis to Gotham City, which is 1000 miles away
    distance_gotham = 1000
    #He then flies to the Fortress of Solitude, which is 2000 miles away from Gotham City
    distance_fortress = 2000
    #Time to fly from Metropolis to Gotham City
    time_gotham = distance_gotham / superman_speed
    #Time to fly from Gotham City to the Fortress of Solitude
    time_fortress = distance_fortress / superman_speed
    #Total time
    total_time = time_gotham + time_fortress
    return total_time
Topic: Serena Williams ### Response:  Question: Serena Williams has 24 Grand Slam titles. 10 of them are in singles, 6 are in doubles, and the rest are in mixed doubles. How many is she missing to beat the all-time record of 31?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena Williams has 24 Grand Slam titles
    grand_slam_titles = 24
    #10 of them are in singles
    singles = 10
    #6 are in doubles
    doubles = 6
    #The rest are in mixed doubles. In mixed doubles, she is missing
    mixed_doubles = grand_slam_titles - singles - doubles
    grand_slam_record = 31
    missing = grand_slam_record - grand_slam_titles
    return missing

Topic: Ninja Turtles ### Response:  Leonardo, Michelangelo, Donatello, and Raphael are the 4 turtles. Leonardo is 20 years old. Michelangelo is 2 years older than Leonardo. Donatello is 4 years older than Michelangelo. Raphael is 10 years older than Donatello. What is the sum of the ages of all 4 turtles?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Leonardo is 20 years old
    leonardo_age = 20
    #Michelangelo is 2 years older than Leonardo
    michelangelo_age = leonardo_age + 2
    #Donatello is 4 years older than Michelangelo
    donatello_age = michelangelo_age + 4
    #Raphael is 10 years older than Donatello
    raphael_age = donatello_age + 10
    #The sum of the ages of all 4 turtles is
    result = leonardo_age + michelangelo_age + donatello_age + raphael_age
    return result

Topic: Taylor Swift ### Response:  Question: Taylor Swift has 2000 toys. She plays with 50 toys a day for 20 days.  She gives 100 toys to her friends. How many toys does she have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Taylor started with 2000 toys
    toys_initial = 2000
    #She played with 50 a day for 20 days
    toys_used_per_day = 50
    #The toys she used are
    toys_used = toys_used_per_day * 20
    #She gave 100 toys to her friends
    toys_given = 100
    #The toys left are
    toys_left = toys_initial - toys_used - toys_given
    return toys_left

Solution:
def solution():

    puzzle_pieces_initial = 200
    #She eats 3 of the pieces
    puzzle_pieces_eaten_kitty = 3
    #Her cat Mikey eats 5
    puzzle_pieces_eaten_mikey = 5
    #The answer is
