How many vibranium shards does she have left?

    costume_repair = 200

    #Shards used for weapon construction
    weapon_construction = 300
    #The answer is

    bad_guys_per_lasso = 10
    #She lassos 10 bad guys on Tuesday
    bad_guys_tuesday = 10
    #20 on Wednesday
    bad_guys_wednesday = 20
    #30 on Thursday
    bad_guys_thursday = 30
    #The answer is

    return result

Topic: Taylor Swift ### Response:  Question: Taylor Swift has 200 cars. 20 of them are black, 50 of them are white, 40 of them are red, and the rest are blue. How many of them are blue?
Solution:

    #Taylor Swift has 200 cars
    total_cars = 200
    #20 of them are black
    black_cars = 20
    #50 of them are white
    white_cars = 50
    #40 of them are red
    red_cars = 40
    #The rest are blue. The answer is
    blue_cars = total_cars - black_cars - white_cars - red_cars

Topic: Thor, the God of Thunder ### Response:  Question: As a part of his training, Thor is lifting 100-pound weights. He lifts 10 weights on Monday, 14 on Tuesday, and 12 on Wednesday. How much weight does he have left to lift this week?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Thor is lifting 100-pound weights
    weight = 100
    #He lifts 10 weights on Monday, 14 on Tuesday, and 12 on Wednesday
    weights_monday = 10
    weights_tuesday = 14
    weights_wednesday = 12
    #The answer is
    result = weight * (5 - weights_monday - weights_tuesday - weights_wednesday)
    return result
Topic: Superman ### Response:  Question: Superman can leap 1000 feet in a single bound. 
If he leaps 1000 feet 5 times in a row, how many miles has he travelled?
Solution:
# 1 mile is 5280 feet
def solution():
    feet_per_leap = 1000
    leaps = 5
    feet_per_mile = 5280
    miles = (feet_per_leap * leaps) / feet_per_mile
    return miles

Topic: Spiderman ### Response:  Question: Spiderman is a superhero. He has 15 spiderwebs. He uses 2 spiderwebs to swing from the top of a building to the bottom of a building. He does this 3 times. How many spiderwebs does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Spiderman started with 15 spiderwebs
    spiderwebs_initial = 15
    #He uses 2 spiderwebs to swing from the top of a building to the bottom of a building
    spiderwebs_per_swing = 2
    #He does this 3 times
    num_swings = 3
    #The spiderwebs he used are
    spiderwebs_used = spiderwebs_per_swing * num_swings
    #Spiderman has spiderwebs left
    spiderwebs_left = spiderwebs_initial - spiderwebs_used
    return spiderwebs_left

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response:  Question: 25 Brontosaurs weigh 2000 pounds each. 20 Stegosauruses weigh 1500 pounds each. 15 T-Rexes weigh 5000 pounds each. How much do all of the dinosaurs weigh?
Solution:
def solution():
    #25 Brontosaurs weigh 2000 pounds each
    brontosaur_weight = 2000
    brontosaur_count = 25
    #20 Stegosauruses weigh 1500 pounds each
    stegosaurus_weight = 1500
    stegosaurus_count = 20
    #15 T-Rexes weigh 5000 pounds each
    t_rex_weight = 5000
    t_rex_count = 15
    #The total weight is
    result = (brontosaur_weight * brontosaur_count) + (stegosaurus_weight * stegosaurus_count) + (t_rex_weight * t_rex_count)
    return result

Topic: unicorns ### Response:  Question: 

Imagine a herd of 100 unicorns. 

- 20% of the unicorns are pink. 
- 70% of the unicorns are blue. 
- 10% of the unicorns are rainbow. 

How many unicorns are not rainbow?

Solution: 

def solution():

    #Total number of unicorns
    total_unicorns = 100

    #Percentage of pink, blue, and rainbow unicorns
    pink_perc = 0.20
    blue_perc = 0.70
    rainbow_perc = 0.10

    #Number of pink, blue, and rainbow unicorns
    pink_unicorns = total_unicorns * pink_perc
    blue_unicorns = total_unicorns * blue_perc
    rainbow_unicorns = total_unicorns * rainbow_perc

    #Number of unicorns that are not rainbow
    not_rainbow_unicorns = total_unicorns - rainbow_unicorns

    return not_rainbow_unicorns

Topic: Iron Man ### Response:  Question: Iron Man has 4000 nuts and bolts. He uses 2000 of them to build a suit of armor. He then uses 1/4 of the remaining nuts and bolts to build a suitcase. How many nuts and bolts does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man has 4000 nuts and bolts
    nuts_bolts = 4000
    #He uses 2000 of them to build a suit of armor
    used_for_armour = 2000
    #He then uses 1/4 of the remaining nuts and bolts to build a suitcase
    used_for_suitcase = (nuts_bolts - used_for_armour) / 4
    #The answer is
    result = nuts_bolts - used_for_armour - used_for_suitcase
    return result

Topic: Spiderman ### Response:  Question: Spiderman can web-sling 300 feet per second. He used his web-slinging to swing from the top of the Empire State Building to the top of the Statue of Liberty. The Empire State Building is 1,250 feet tall. The Statue of Liberty is 305 feet tall. If it takes 5 seconds to swing from the Empire State Building to the Statue of Liberty, how far, in feet, did Spiderman swing?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Spiderman can web-sling 300 feet per second
    web_sling_speed = 300
    #He used his web-slinging to swing from the top of the Empire State Building to the top of the Statue of Liberty.
    #The Empire State Building is 1,250 feet tall.
    empire_state_building_height = 1250
    #The Statue of Liberty is 305 feet tall.
    statue_of_liberty_height = 305
    #If it takes 5 seconds to swing from the Empire State Building to the Statue of Liberty,
    time = 5
    #The answer is
    result = (empire_state_building_height - statue_of_liberty_height) / time
    return result

Topic: field hockey ### Response: 12 players on a field hockey team are splitting 200 cones. 20 of the cones are used to make a circle for the goal. 40 of the cones are used to make a semicircle for each player. How many cones are left for the goalies?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total cones
    cones_total = 200
    #Cones used for goal
    cones_goal = 20
    #Cones used for semicircle for each player
    cones_player = 40
    #Cones left for goalies
    cones_goalies = cones_total - cones_goal - cones_player
    return cones_goalies

Topic: Serena Williams ### Response: 1. Question: Serena has 23 Grand Slam titles. 3 of them are from the French Open. 5 of them are from Wimbledon. 2 of them are from the Australian Open. 13 of them are from the US Open. How many US Open titles does Serena have?
2. Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena has 23 Grand Slam titles
    grand_slam_titles = 23
    #3 of them are from the French Open
    french_open_titles = 3
    #5 of them are from Wimbledon
    wimbledon_titles = 5
    #2 of them are from the Australian Open

    #13 of them are from the US Open

Topic: unicorns ### Response:  Question: What is the least number of unicorn horns I need to collect to ride 2 unicorns that each require 3 horns and have 1 horn left over for my friend?
Solution:
def solution():
    #I need to ride 2 unicorns
    unicorns = 2
    #Each unicorn requires 3 horns
    horns_per_unicorn = 3
    #I also need 1 horn for my friend
    horns_friend = 1
    #The total number of horns I need is
    result = horns_per_unicorn * unicorns + horns_friend
    return result

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: Timmy and Tommy both like ice cream. Timmy can eat 4 scoops of ice cream. Tommy can eat twice as much as Timmy. 

How many scoops of ice cream can they both eat?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Timmy can eat 4 scoops of ice cream
    timmy_scoops = 4
    #Tommy can eat twice as much as Timmy
    tommy_scoops = 2 * timmy_scoops
    #The answer is
    result = timmy_scoops + tommy_scoops
    return result
Topic: soccer ### Response:  Question: 10 members of the soccer team are in the starting lineup. 2 of them are forwards, 3 of them are midfielders, and the rest are defenders. How many are defenders?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total members in the starting lineup
    total_members = 10
    #Members in the forwards and midfielders
    forwards_and_midfielders = 2 + 3
    #The rest are defenders
    defenders = total_members - forwards_and_midfielders
    return defenders

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response:  Question: There were 200 million dinosaurs on the planet 200 million years ago. 50 million years later, 150 million of them were extinct. 25 million more dinosaurs became extinct 50 million years after that. How many dinosaurs were left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The number of dinosaurs at the beginning
    dinosaurs_initial = 200000000
    #50 million years later, 150 million of them were extinct
    dinosaurs_extinct_1 = 150000000
    #25 million more dinosaurs became extinct 50 million years after that
    dinosaurs_extinct_2 = 25000000
    #The answer is
    result = dinosaurs_initial - dinosaurs_extinct_1 - dinosaurs_extinct_2
    return result

Topic: Fortnite ### Response:  Question: There were 1000 players in a Fortnite match. 100 of them were eliminated in the first 5 minutes. 200 more were eliminated in the next 5 minutes. 1/2 of the remaining players were eliminated in the next 5 minutes. How many players are left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total players
    players = 1000
    #100 of them were eliminated in the first 5 minutes
    eliminated_1 = 100
    #200 more were eliminated in the next 5 minutes
    eliminated_2 = 200
    #1/2 of the remaining players were eliminated in the next 5 minutes
    eliminated_3 = 1/2 * (players - eliminated_1 - eliminated_2)
    #The answer is
    result = players - eliminated_1 - eliminated_2 - eliminated_3
    return result

Topic: swimming ### Response:  Question: 
There are 10 fish in the aquarium. Two-thirds of the fish are in the main aquarium and the rest are in the smaller aquarium. How many fish are in the smaller aquarium?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of fish
    total_fish = 10
    #Two-thirds of the fish are in the main aquarium
    fish_in_main_aquarium = 2/3 * total_fish
    #The rest are in the smaller aquarium
    fish_in_smaller_aquarium = total_fish - fish_in_main_aquarium
    #The answer is
    result = fish_in_smaller_aquarium
    return result

Topic: football ### Response:  Question: 4000 people attended the Super Bowl. 1500 of them were from the winning team. 2500 of them were from the losing team. How many people were from other teams?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total attendees
    total_attendees = 4000
    #Winning team attendees
    winning_team_attendees = 1500
    #Losing team attendees
    losing_team_attendees = 2500
    #Other team attendees is
    other_team_attendees = total_attendees - winning_team_attendees - losing_team_attendees
    return other_team_attendees
Topic: Minecraft ### Response:  Question: 3000 Minecraft blocks are in a build. 1000 of the blocks are in a house. 500 of the blocks are in a garden. 200 of the blocks are in a pool. 50 of the blocks are in a mine. How many blocks are not in any of these builds?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of blocks
    total_blocks = 3000
    #Number of blocks in the house
    blocks_in_house = 1000
    #Number of blocks in the garden
    blocks_in_garden = 500
    #Number of blocks in the pool
    blocks_in_pool = 200
    #Number of blocks in the mine
    blocks_in_mine = 50
    #Number of blocks not in any of these builds is
    blocks_not_in_builds = total_blocks - blocks_in_house - blocks_in_garden - blocks_in_pool - blocks_in_mine
    return blocks_not_in_builds
Topic: pizza ### Response:  Question: 2 boxes of pizza have 4 slices each. If 18 people eat 3 slices each, how many slices of pizza are left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #2 boxes of pizza have 4 slices each
    pizza_slices_per_box = 2 * 4
    #18 people eat 3 slices each
    people = 18
    slices_per_person = 3
    #The total number of slices eaten is
    total_slices_eaten = people * slices_per_person
    #The number of slices left is
    slices_left = pizza_slices_per_box - total_slices_eaten
    return slices_left

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: 200 scoops of ice cream are on the conveyor belt. 100 scoops are chocolate, 50 scoops are vanilla, and the rest are strawberry. If 50 scoops are strawberry, how many scoops of ice cream are not strawberry?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total scoops of ice cream
    total_scoops = 200
    #Scoops of chocolate and vanilla ice cream
    chocolate_scoops = 100
    vanilla_scoops = 50
    #Scoops of strawberry ice cream
    strawberry_scoops = total_scoops - chocolate_scoops - vanilla_scoops
    #Scoops of ice cream that are not strawberry
    scoops_not_strawberry = total_scoops - strawberry_scoops
    return scoops_not_strawberry

    minutes_per_game = 48
    #There are 4 quarters in a game, each 12 minutes long
    minutes_per_quarter = 12

    full_quarters_per_game = 4
    #The rest of the time is the overtime
    overtime_per_game = minutes_per_game - (full_quarters_per_game * minutes_per_quarter)
    #There are 82 regular season games in a year
    games_per_season = 82
    #The total time he will spend on the court in the 2023-2024 season
    total_minutes = season * games_per_season * minutes_per_game
    #Each 60 minutes makes

    brontosaurus_length = 20
    #The stegosaurus is 15 feet long
    stegosaurus_length = 15
    #The number of stegosaurs necessary to be as long as a brontosaurus

    followers_initial = 5000
    #New followers a day
    new_followers_per_day = 2000
    #Followers lost a day
    followers_lost_per_day = 500
    #Followers after 5 days

Topic: Batman ### Response: 1. Batman is at a convenience store. He buys 5 sodas and 6 candy bars. 2. He has 20 dollars. 3. Sodas are 2 dollars each and candy bars are 3 dollars each. 4. How much money does he have left?

def solution():  # 1.
    sodas = 5
    candy_bars = 6
    # 2.
    initial_money = 20
    # 3.
    soda_price = 2
    candy_bar_price = 3
    # 4.
    spent_money = sodas * soda_price + candy_bars * candy_bar_price
    money_left = initial_money - spent_money
    return money_left

Topic: Batman ### Response:  Question: Batman is a superhero. He has 40 gadgets. 20 of them are in the Batcave. 10 of them are in the Batmobile. 5 of them are in the Batwing. 5 of them are on his person. How many gadgets does he have on his person?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Batman has 40 gadgets
    gadgets_total = 40
    #20 of them are in the Batcave
    gadgets_batcave = 20
    #10 of them are in the Batmobile
    gadgets_batmobile = 10
    #5 of them are in the Batwing
    gadgets_batwing = 5
    #5 of them are on his person
    gadgets_person = 5
    #The answer is
    result = gadgets_total - gadgets_batcave - gadgets_batmobile - gadgets_batwing
    return result
Topic: Ninja Turtles ### Response: 4 turtles: Michelangelo, Donatello, Leonardo, and Raphael. Raphael is 5 years older than Donatello. Leonardo is 2 years younger than Michelangelo. 

def solution():
    #Leonardo is 2 years younger than Michelangelo.
    leonardo_age = 14
    michelangelo_age = leonardo_age + 2
    #Raphael is 5 years older than Donatello.
    raphael_age = 16
    donatello_age = raphael_age - 5
    #The average age of the turtles is
    average_age = (michelangelo_age + donatello_age + leonardo_age + raphael_age) / 4
    return average_age

Topic: Taylor Swift ### Response:  Question: Taylor Swift is 13. Her 10-year-old brother is 4 years younger than she is. Her 15-year-old sister is 2 years older than her. How old is the average age of the 3 siblings?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Taylor Swift is 13
    taylor_age = 13
    #Her 10-year-old brother is 4 years younger than she is
    brother_age = taylor_age - 4
    #Her 15-year-old sister is 2 years older than her
    sister_age = taylor_age + 2
    #The average age of the 3 siblings
    average_age = (taylor_age + brother_age + sister_age) / 3
    return average_age

    return result

Topic: Power Rangers ### Response: 

Question: 

Jason, the Red Ranger, has 1500 zords. Zack, the Blue Ranger, has 1200 zords. Kimber, the Yellow Ranger, has 1250 zords. Trini, the Pink Ranger, has 1375 zords. How many zords does the Power Rangers need to defeat the Putties
Topic: cars ### Response:  Question: There are 1000 cars in a parking lot. A fifth of the cars are Teslas. A third of the Teslas are white. How many of the Teslas are white?
Solution:
def solution():
    #There are 1000 cars in a parking lot
    cars = 1000
    #A fifth of the cars are Teslas
    teslas = cars / 5
    #A third of the Teslas are white
    white_teslas = teslas / 3
    #The answer is
    result = white_teslas
    return result

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: 
Alice, Bob, and Charlie went to the ice cream shop. Alice bought 3 scoops of ice cream, Bob bought 2 scoops of ice cream, and Charlie bought 4 scoops of ice cream. How many scoops of ice cream did they buy in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Alice bought 3 scoops of ice cream
    alice_scoops = 3
    #Bob bought 2 scoops of ice cream
    bob_scoops = 2
    #Charlie bought 4 scoops of ice cream
    charlie_scoops = 4
    #The answer is
    result = alice_scoops + bob_scoops + charlie_scoops
    return result

Topic: cars ### Response:  Question: 100 cars are in a parking lot. It costs $10 to charge an EV, and $5 to charge a hybrid. 70% of the cars are EVs, and 20% are hybrids. How much does it cost to charge all the cars?
Solution:
def solution():
    #100 cars are in a parking lot
    total_cars = 100
    #70% of the cars are EVs
    ev_percentage = 0.7
    #20% are hybrids
    hybrid_percentage = 0.2
    #It costs $10 to charge an EV, and $5 to charge a hybrid
    ev_cost = 10
    hybrid_cost = 5
    #The total cost is
    ev_cars = total_cars * ev_percentage
    hybrid_cars = total_cars * hybrid_percentage
    ev_cost_total = ev_cars * ev_cost
    hybrid_cost_total = hybrid_cars * hybrid_cost
    total_cost = ev_cost_total + hybrid_cost_total
    return total_cost

Topic: soccer ### Response:  Question: 22 soccer players on a team. 8 of them are forwards, 6 are midfielders, and the rest are defenders. How many are defenders?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total soccer players
    total_players = 22
    #Forwards
    forwards = 8
    #Midfielders
    midfielders = 6
    #Defenders
    defenders = total_players - forwards - midfielders
    return defenders
Topic: cheer leading ### Response:  Question: There were 50 people at the pep rally. 10 of the people were the cheerleaders. 20 of the people were the football players. 10 of the people were the band. 5 of the people were the faculty. The rest of the people were the students. How many of the people were students?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total people
    total_people = 50
    #Cheerleaders
    cheerleaders = 10
    #Football players
    football_players = 20
    #Band
    band = 10
    #Faculty
    faculty = 5
    #The rest are students
    students = total_people - cheerleaders - football_players - band - faculty
    return students

Topic: Pokémon ### Response:  Question: Ash Ketchum, the Pokémon trainer, has 50 Pokéballs. He uses 10 of them to catch 10 Pikachu. He then uses 5 of them to catch 5 Squirtle. How many Pokéballs does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Ash started with 50 Pokéballs
    pokeballs_initial = 50
    #He used 10 of them to catch 10 Pikachu
    pokeballs_used_pikachu = 10
    #He used 5 of them to catch 5 Squirtle
    pokeballs_used_squirtle = 5
    #The answer is
    result = pokeballs_initial - pokeballs_used_pikachu - pokeballs_used_squirtle
    return result
Topic: Wonder Woman ### Response:  Wonder Woman is a superhero.  She can lasso the truth, she is a great athlete, and she is a skilled combatant.  She has 100 lassos.  She uses 30 lassos to lasso the truth and 50 lassos to capture criminals.  How many lassos does she have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Wonder Woman's total lassos
    total_lassos = 100
    #Lassos used for lassoing the truth
    lassos_lassoing = 30
    #Lassos used for capturing criminals
    lassos_capturing = 50
    #The answer is
    lassos_left = total_lassos - lassos_lassoing - lassos_capturing
    return lassos_left

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: 30 people in a class each get 3 scoops of ice cream. 
Each scoop is 150 ml. 
How many liters of ice cream do they have in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #30 people in a class
    people = 30
    #Each get 3 scoops of ice cream
    scoops = 3
    #Each scoop is 150 ml
    ml_per_scoop = 150
    #The answer is in liters
    ml_to_liters = 1000
    #Total ml of ice cream
    total_ml = people * scoops * ml_per_scoop
    #Convert to liters
    total_liters = total_ml / ml_to_liters
    #The answer is
    result = total_liters
    return result
Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response:  Question:  In a 24-hour period, Captain Marvel can punch 3600 times. 
She punches 200 times per hour for the first 6 hours. 
Then, she punches 250 times per hour for the next 8 hours. 
After that, she punches 300 times per hour for the last 10 hours. 
How many punches does she throw in a 30-day period?
Solution:
def solution():
    punches_per_day = 3600
    days = 30
    punches = punches_per_day * days
    return punches

Topic: Taylor Swift ### Response:  Question: Taylor Swift has 2000 albums. 500 of them are in the pop genre, 500 of them are in the country genre, 500 of them are in the rock genre, and 500 of them are in the folk genre. How many of her albums are not in the pop, country, rock, or folk genre?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total albums
    total_albums = 2000
    #Pop genre albums
    pop_genre_albums = 500
    #Country genre albums
    country_genre_albums = 500
    #Rock genre albums
    rock_genre_albums = 500
    #Folk genre albums
    folk_genre_albums = 500
    #Non-genre albums
    non_genre_albums = total_albums - pop_genre_albums - country_genre_albums - rock_genre_albums - folk_genre_albums
    return non_genre_albums

Topic: field hockey ### Response:  Question: In a field hockey match, each team has 11 players. 2 of the players are in goal, 3 are in defense, 4 are in midfield, and the rest are in attack. How many players are in attack?
Solution:
def solution():
    #In a field hockey match, each team has 11 players
    team_size = 11
    #2 of the players are in goal
    players_goal = 2
    #3 are in defense
    players_defense = 3
    #4 are in midfield
    players_midfield = 4
    #The rest of the players are in attack
    players_attack = team_size - players_goal - players_defense - players_midfield
    return players_attack
Topic: field hockey ### Response:  Question: 2009 field hockeysticks were made. 1/10 of them are too short, 1/5 of them are too long, and 3/5 of the rest are just right. How many field hockey sticks are just right?
Solution:
def solution():
    #2009 field hockey sticks were made
    hockey_sticks = 2009
    #1/10 of them are too short
    too_short = hockey_sticks / 10
    #1/5 of them are too long
    too_long = hockey_sticks / 5
    #3/5 of the rest are just right
    just_right = (hockey_sticks - too_short - too_long) * 3 / 5
    #The answer is
    result = int(just_right)
    return result

Topic: trains ### Response:  Question: 15 passenger trains can hold 20 passengers. 30 freight trains can hold 40 passengers. How many total passengers can these trains hold?
Solution:
def solution():
    #15 passenger trains can hold 20 passengers each
    passenger_trains = 15
    passengers_per_train = 20
    #30 freight trains can hold 40 passengers each
    freight_trains = 30
    passengers_per_freight_train = 40
    #The total passengers is
    total_passengers = (passenger_trains * passengers_per_train) + (freight_trains * passengers_per_freight_train)
    return total_passengers
Topic: Superman ### Response:  Question:  
Superman is 1000 times stronger than a normal human. A normal human can lift 300 pounds. How many pounds can Superman lift?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A normal human can lift 300 pounds
    human_lift = 300
    #Superman is 1000 times stronger
    superman_strength = 1000
    #The answer is
    superman_lift = human_lift * superman_strength
    return superman_lift

Topic: Minecraft ### Response:  Question: A Minecraft player is in a 1000 block long minecart. The minecart can travel 1000 blocks in 10 minutes. How many blocks can it travel in 5 minutes?
Solution:

    return result

Topic: Patrick Mahomes ### Response:  Question: Patrick Mahomes is the quarterback for the Kansas City Chiefs. He has 1250 passing yards. 250 of the yards are from the 1st quarter, 500 are from the 2nd quarter, and 500 are from the 3rd quarter. How many yards does he have left for the 4th quarter?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Patrick Mahomes has 1250 passing yards
    total_yards = 1250
    #250 of the yards are from the 1st quarter
    yards_1st_quarter = 250
    #500 are from the 2nd quarter
    yards_2nd_quarter = 500
    #500 are from the 3rd quarter
    yards_3rd_quarter = 500
    #The yards left for the 4th quarter is
    result = total_yards - (yards_1st_quarter + yards_2nd_quarter + yards_3rd_quarter)
    return result

    #He flies for 1.5 hours

    #The answer is

    return result

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total players on each team
    total_players = 12
    #Setters
    setters = 2
    #Hitters
    hitters = 4
    #The rest are blockers. The answer is
    result = total_players - setters - hitters
    return result

    sticks_initial = 300
    #She is buying 50 more sticks
    sticks_bought = 50
    #She is giving 120 to her teammates

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total players
    total_players = 12
    #Setters
    setters = 2
    #Outside hitters
    outside_hitters = 3
    #Middles
    middles = 3
    #Blockers
    blockers = 2
    #Defenders are the rest

    return defenders

Topic: planes ### Response:  Question: A 747 can seat 566 people. A 777 can seat 346 people. 747s and 777s were parked at an airport. 10 747s and 8 777s were parked. How many people can the planes seat?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A 747 can seat 566 people
    seats_747 = 566
    #A 777 can seat 346 people
    seats_777 = 346
    #10 747s and 8 777s were parked
    planes_747 = 10
    planes_777 = 8
    #The answer is
    result = (seats_747 * planes_747) + (seats_777 * planes_777)
    return result

    total_dogs = 10
    #5 of them are dachshunds
    dachshunds = 5
    #2 of them are poodles
    poodles = 2
    #The rest are corgis
    corgis = total_dogs - dachshunds - poodles

    return result
Topic: dinosaurs ### Response:  Question: A T-Rex weighs 20,000 pounds. A brontosaurus weighs 3 times as much. How many T-Rexes would it take to weigh as much as a brontosaurus?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A T-Rex weighs 20,000 pounds
    t_rex_weight = 20000
    #A brontosaurus weighs 3 times as much
    brontosaurus_weight = 3 * t_rex_weight
    #The answer is
    result = brontosaurus_weight / t_rex_weight
    return result

    #Elsa has 5000 scoops of ice cream
    total_scoops = 5000
    #2000 of them are chocolate
    chocolate = 2000
    #1500 of them are vanilla
    vanilla = 1500
    #500 of them are strawberry
    strawberry = 500
    #The answer is
    result = (chocolate + vanilla) - strawberry
    return result

Topic: Black Panther ### Response:  Question: Black Panther can outrun a cheetah. He can run 1000 feet per second. A cheetah can run 500 feet per second. How many seconds does he have to spare to outrun a cheetah in a 5000-foot-long race?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Black Panther can run 1000 feet per second
    black_panther_speed = 1000
    #A cheetah can run 500 feet per second
    cheetah_speed = 500
    #The race is 5000 feet long
    race_length = 5000
    #Black Panther's time to complete the race
    black_panther_time = race_length / black_panther_speed
    #Cheetah's time to complete the race
    cheetah_time = race_length / cheetah_speed
    #The answer is
    result = cheetah_time - black_panther_time
    return result

Topic: field hockey ### Response:  Question: In field hockey, each team has 11 players on the field at a time. If a total of 44 players are on the field, including the 11 on each team, how many games are being played at the same time?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Each team has 11 players on the field
    players_per_team = 11
    #Total players on the field
    total_players = 44
    #The answer is
    result = total_players / (2 * players_per_team)
    return result

Topic: Patrick Mahomes ### Response: 1. What is Patrick Mahomes' total net worth in 2022? (In millions of dollars) 
def solution():
    #Patrick Mahomes is an American football quarterback. 
    #He has a 10-year, $503 million contract with the Kansas City Chiefs. 
    #He also has a Nike endorsement deal worth $1 million per year. 
    #In 2022, he will be 26 years old. 
    #At that age, the average NFL quarterback makes $20 million per year. 
    #His total net worth in 2022 is: 
    #Contract earnings + Nike endorsement + Average NFL quarterback salary
    result = (503*12*10) + (1*12*26) + (20*12*26)
    return result

Topic: Spiderman ### Response:  Question: Spiderman has 100 spiderwebs. He uses 20 spiderwebs to capture a criminal. He uses 30 spiderwebs to save a cat. He uses 50 spiderwebs to stop a bank robbery. How many spiderwebs does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Spiderman has 100 spiderwebs
    spiderwebs = 100
    #He uses 20 to capture a criminal
    spiderwebs_used_criminal = 20
    #He uses 30 to save a cat
    spiderwebs_used_cat = 30
    #He uses 50 to stop a bank robbery
    spiderwebs_used_bank = 50
    #The answer is
    result = spiderwebs - spiderwebs_used_criminal - spiderwebs_used_cat - spiderwebs_used_bank
    return result

Topic: Thor, the God of Thunder ### Response:  Question: Thor has to travel to 5000 worlds. Each world has 2000 inhabitants. He can only carry 1000 inhabitants per world. How many trips does he have to make?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of worlds
    total_worlds = 5000
    #Number of inhabitants in each world
    inhabitants_per_world = 2000
    #Thor can carry 1000 inhabitants per world
    thor_capacity = 1000
    #The total capacity of worlds Thor can carry is
    total_capacity = thor_capacity * total_worlds
    #The total number of inhabitants is
    total_inhabitants = total_worlds * inhabitants_per_world
    #The number of trips he has to make is
    trips = total_inhabitants // total_capacity
    return trips
Topic: cats ### Response:  Question: There are 12 cats in a cat park. 80% of them are black, 10% are white, and the rest are gray. How many gray cats are there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total cats
    total_cats = 12
    #80% of them are black
    black_cats = total_cats * 0.8
    #10% are white
    white_cats = total_cats * 0.1
    #The rest are gray
    gray_cats = total_cats - black_cats - white_cats
    return gray_cats

    unicorns_initial = 25
    #10 of the unicorns are pink
    unicorns_pink = 10

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: 10 scoops of ice cream weigh 4.5 pounds. 1 scoop of ice cream weighs 1/270 of a pound. 30 people order 2 scoops of ice cream each. How many pounds of ice cream do they need to order?
Solution:
def solution():
    #10 scoops of ice cream weigh 4.5 pounds
    ice_cream_10_scoops = 4.5
    #1 scoop of ice cream weighs 1/270 of a pound
    ice_cream_1_scoop = 1/270
    #30 people order 2 scoops of ice cream each
    people = 30
    scoops_per_person = 2
    #The answer is
    result = ice_cream_1_scoop * scoops_per_person * people
    return result

Topic: Super Mario ### Response:  Question: In the video game Super Mario, Mario has to rescue the Princess. 2000 coins are required to rescue the Princess. 500 of the coins are in the Mushroom Kingdom. 300 of the coins are in the Koopa Kingdom. 200 of the coins are in the Star Kingdom.  How many of the coins are in the Fire Kingdom?
Solution:
def solution():
    #2000 coins are required to rescue the Princess
    coins_total = 2000
    #500 of the coins are in the Mushroom Kingdom
    coins_mushroom = 500
    #300 of the coins are in the Koopa Kingdom
    coins_koopa = 300
    #200 of the coins are in the Star Kingdom
    coins_star = 200
    #The answer is
    result = coins_total - coins_mushroom - coins_koopa - coins_star
    return result

Topic: Iron Man ### Response:  Iron Man's suit of armor is made of 2000 individual pieces. 500 of the pieces are in his head. 1000 of the pieces are in the rest of his body. 500 of the pieces are in his legs. How many pieces are in his hands and feet?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man's suit of armor is made of 2000 individual pieces
    total_pieces = 2000
    #500 of the pieces are in his head
    head_pieces = 500
    #1000 of the pieces are in the rest of his body
    body_pieces = 1000
    #500 of the pieces are in his legs
    leg_pieces = 500
    #The answer is
    result = total_pieces - head_pieces - body_pieces - leg_pieces
    return result
Topic: Superman ### Response:  Question: Superman is 8.5 feet tall. 2000 people are 5.5 feet tall. How much taller is Superman than the average person?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman is 8.5 feet tall
    superman_height = 8.5
    #2000 people are 5.5 feet tall
    people_height = 2000 * 5.5
    #The average height is
    average_height = (superman_height + people_height) / 2001
    #Superman is
    result = superman_height - average_height
    return result

100 of the scoops were chocolate, 

200 of the scoops were vanilla, and 

100 of the scoops were strawberry. 

How many of the scoops were not strawberry?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total scoops
    total_scoops = 300
    #Scoops of chocolate
    chocolate_scoops = 100
    #Scoops of vanilla
    vanilla_scoops = 200
    #Scoops of strawberry
    strawberry_scoops = 100

Topic: Naruto ### Response:  Naruto is a ninja. He can run 10 kilometers in 20 minutes. 1 kilometer is 1000 meters. How many meters can he run in 1 hour? 
def solution():
    # Naruto can run 10 kilometers in 20 minutes
    distance_in_kilometers = 10
    time_in_minutes = 20
    # 1 kilometer is 1000 meters
    kilometers_to_meters = 1000
    # Naruto can run 10 kilometers
    total_distance = distance_in_kilometers * kilometers_to_meters
    # in 1 hour, which is 60 minutes
    time_in_hours = time_in_minutes * 60
    # The answer is
    result = total_distance / time_in_hours
    return result

    #3 more 49ers players are in the game, but on the sidelines

Topic: dogs ### Response:  Question: 5000 dogs in a city have a collar, and 12000 do not. 40% of the dogs with a collar and 10% of the dogs without a collar are in a dog park. How many dogs in the city are in a dog park?
Solution:
def solution():
    #5000 dogs in a city have a collar
    collar_population = 5000
    #12000 do not have a collar
    no_collar_population = 12000
    #40% of the dogs with a collar are in a dog park
    collar_in_park = 0.4 * collar_population
    #10% of the dogs without a collar are in a dog park
    no_collar_in_park = 0.1 * no_collar_population
    #The answer is
    result = collar_in_park + no_collar_in_park
    return result

Topic: cheer leading ### Response:  Question: There are 24 students in a cheer leading squad. 1/4 of them are in 6th grade, 1/2 of them are in 7th grade, and the rest are in 8th grade. How many of them are in 8th grade?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total students
    total_students = 24
    #1/4 of them are in 6th grade
    students_6th_grade = total_students / 4
    #1/2 of them are in 7th grade
    students_7th_grade = total_students / 2
    #The rest are in 8th grade
    students_8th_grade = total_students - students_6th_grade - students_7th_grade
    return students_8th_grade

Topic: field hockey ### Response:  Question: In field hockey, a goal is worth 1 point. A tie game is 0 points for each team. If 2 games are played and 1 ends in a tie with a score of 2-2 and the other game is won by Team A with a score of 3-0, what is the total score for both games?
Solution:
def solution():
    #In field hockey, a goal is worth 1 point
    goal_point = 1
    #A tie game is 0 points for each team
    tie_game_points = 0
    #If 2 games are played and 1 ends in a tie with a score of 2-2
    tie_game_score = tie_game_points + (2 * goal_point) + (2 * goal_point)
    #and the other game is won by Team A with a score of 3-0
    win_game_score = (3 * goal_point) + (0 * goal_point)
    #The total score for both games is
    total_score = tie_game_score + win_game_score
    return total_score
Topic: Power Rangers ### Response:  Question: The Power Rangers are a group of 5 superheroes. 1 of them is 18 years old. 2 of them are 17 years old. 2 of them are 16 years old. What is the average age of the Power Rangers?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The Power Rangers are a group of 5 superheroes
    rangers_total = 5
    #1 of them is 18 years old
    rangers_18 = 1
    #2 of them are 17 years old
    rangers_17 = 2
    #2 of them are 16 years old
    rangers_16 = 2
    #Their ages are
    ages = rangers_18 * 18 + rangers_17 * 17 + rangers_16 * 16
    #The answer is
    result = ages / rangers_total
    return result

Topic: Minecraft ### Response:  Question: In Minecraft, a Creeper is a hostile mob that, when it explodes, can destroy 50 blocks of stone. 

If 20 Creepers explode in a 100-block-long stone mine, how many blocks of stone are left?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Number of Creepers
    creepers = 20
    #Number of blocks of stone per Creeper
    stone_per_creeper = 50
    #Total number of blocks of stone in the mine
    total_stone = 100
    #Number of blocks of stone left after the Creepers explode
    stone_left = total_stone - creepers * stone_per_creeper
    return stone_left
Topic: Black Panther ### Response:  Question: Black Panther has 30 vibranium-powered cars. The Wakandan government buys 500 more vibranium-powered cars. If each car has 20 vibranium crystals, how many vibranium crystals does Black Panther have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Black Panther started with 30 vibranium-powered cars
    cars_initial = 30
    #The government bought 500 more
    cars_bought = 500
    #Each car has 20 vibranium crystals
    crystals_per_car = 20
    #The answer is
    result = (cars_initial + cars_bought) * crystals_per_car
    return result

Topic: cars ### Response:  Question: 

Jules owns 25 cars. 10 of them are sports cars, and 5 of them are convertibles. 3 of the sports cars are also convertibles. How many of the cars are neither sports cars nor convertibles?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total cars
    total_cars = 25
    #Sports cars
    sports_cars = 10
    #Convertibles
    convertibles = 5
    #Sports cars that are also convertibles
    sports_convertibles = 3
    #Cars that are neither sports cars nor convertibles
    neither = total_cars - sports_cars - convertibles + sports_convertibles
    return neither

    grand_slam_titles = 14
    #6 of them are in singles

    #The rest are in mixed doubles

    children = 500
    #Total adults
    adults = 200
    #Total scoops of ice cream given to children
    scoops_children = children * 2
    #Total scoops of ice cream given to adults

Topic: lacrosse ### Response:  Question: A lacrosse team has 12 players. 8 of the players are short, 3 are tall, and the rest are average height. If 2 of the short players are also average height, how many players are not short?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total players
    total_players = 12
    #Short players
    short_players = 8
    #Tall players
    tall_players = 3
    #Average height players
    average_height_players = total_players - short_players - tall_players
    #2 of the short players are also average height
    short_and_average_height_players = 2
    #Players who are not short
    result = total_players - short_players + short_and_average_height_players
    return result

Topic: Spiderman ### Response:  Question:  Spiderman has 5000 webshooters. He uses 20% of them to fight crime on Tuesday, 3000 more on Wednesday, and 1000 more on Thursday. How many webshooters does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Spiderman started with 5000 webshooters
    webshooters_initial = 5000
    #20% of them, which is 1000, he used on Tuesday
    webshooters_used_tuesday = 5000 * 0.2
    #He used 3000 more on Wednesday
    webshooters_used_wednesday = 3000
    #And 1000 more on Thursday
    webshooters_used_thursday = 1000
    #The answer is
    result = webshooters_initial - webshooters_used_tuesday - webshooters_used_wednesday - webshooters_used_thursday
    return result

Topic: cheer leading ### Response:  Question: On Monday, a cheerleader has 32 teethbrushes. On Tuesday, she has 2 more. On Wednesday, she has 10 more. On Thursday, she has 22. On Friday, she has 5 less. How many teethbrushes does she have at the end of the week?
Solution:
def solution():
    #On Monday, a cheerleader has 32 teethbrushes
    teethbrushes_monday = 32
    #On Tuesday, she has 2 more
    teethbrushes_tuesday = teethbrushes_monday + 2
    #On Wednesday, she has 10 more
    teethbrushes_wednesday = teethbrushes_tuesday + 10
    #On Thursday, she has 22
    teethbrushes_thursday = 22
    #On Friday, she has 5 less
    teethbrushes_friday = teethbrushes_thursday - 5
    #The answer is
    result = teethbrushes_monday + teethbrushes_tuesday + teethbrushes_wednesday + teethbrushes_thursday + teethbrushes_friday
    return result

    pikachu = 100
    #50 of them are Squirtle
    squirtle = 50
    #20 of them are Bulbasaur
    bulbasaur = 20
    #30 of them are Charmander
    charmander = 30
    #The answer is
    other_pokemon = total_pokemon - pikachu - squirtle - bulbasaur - charmander
    return other_pokemon

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: In a freezer, there are 20 liters of milk, 15 liters of cream, and 12 liters of sugar.  If you want to make ice cream, how many liters of water do you need?
Solution:

    #We need to make 1 liter of ice cream which is 200ml of milk, 300ml of cream and 400ml of sugar.
    #Therefore, we need 200ml of water to make up the remaining volume.
    water_needed = 200 / 1000
    return water_needed

    #They used 200 to enchant a sword

Topic: Thor, the God of Thunder ### Response:  Question: Thor has 1000 thunderbolts. 250 of them are in his Hammer. 100 of them are in his lightning. 200 of them are in his storms. How many thunderbolts does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Thor has 1000 thunderbolts
    thunderbolts = 1000
    #250 of them are in his Hammer
    thunderbolts_hammer = 250
    #100 of them are in his lightning
    thunderbolts_lightning = 100
    #200 of them are in his storms
    thunderbolts_storms = 200
    #Thunderbolts in Hammer + Lightning + Storms
    result = thunderbolts_hammer + thunderbolts_lightning + thunderbolts_storms
    #Thor has left
    thunderbolts_left = thunderbolts - result
    return thunderbolts_left

Topic: basketball ### Response:  Question: LeBron James, the star of the Lakers, is on a 50-game scoring streak. He scores 40 points in 20 games and 30 points in 30 games. How many points does he need to average 50 points a game for the rest of the season?
Solution:
def solution():
    #LeBron James is on a 50-game scoring streak
    games = 50
    #He scores 40 points in 20 games and 30 points in 30 games
    points_40 = 20 * 40
    points_30 = 30 * 30
    total_points = points_40 + points_30
    #The rest of the games in the season is
    games_left = 82 - games
    #He needs to average 50 points a game for the rest of the season
    points_per_game = 50 * games_left
    #He has already scored
    points_scored = total_points
    #He needs to score
    points_needed = points_per_game - points_scored
    return points_needed

Topic: volleyball ### Response:  Volleyball team has 12 players including a coach. 

Each player has 4 kneepads. 

The coach has 2 kneepads. 

How many kneepads does the team have in total?

Solution:
def solution():
    #The volleyball team has 12 players including a coach
    players = 12
    #Each player has 4 kneepads
    kneepads_per_player = 4
    #The coach has 2 kneepads
    kneepads_coach = 2
    #Total kneepads
    total_kneepads = (players - 1) * kneepads_per_player + kneepads_coach
    return total_kneepads

Topic: field hockey ### Response:  Question: On a particular day, a field hockey team had 412 shots on goal. 200 of the shots were taken by the forwards, 150 of the shots were taken by the midfielders, and the rest of the shots were taken by the defenders. How many shots on goal were taken by the defenders?
Solution:
def solution():
    #On a particular day, a field hockey team had 412 shots on goal
    total_shots = 412
    #200 of the shots were taken by the forwards
    fwd_shots = 200
    #150 of the shots were taken by the midfielders
    mid_shots = 150
    #The rest of the shots were taken by the defenders.
    def_shots = total_shots - fwd_shots - mid_shots
    return def_shots

How much more did Bob's order cost than Alice's order?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Alice's order cost
    alice_order = 2 + 0.50
    #Bob's order cost
    bob_order = 2*2 + 0.50
    #Bob's order cost more than Alice's order
    more_cost = bob_order - alice_order
    return more_cost

Topic: trains ### Response:  Question: 300 trains left the station. 100 of them were headed to the east. 120 of them were headed to the west. 80 of them were headed to the north. The rest of the trains were headed to the south. How many trains were headed to the south?
Solution:
def solution():
    #300 trains left the station
    trains_total = 300
    #100 of them were headed to the east
    trains_east = 100
    #120 of them were headed to the west
    trains_west = 120
    #80 of them were headed to the north
    trains_north = 80
    #The rest of the trains were headed to the south
    trains_south = trains_total - trains_east - trains_west - trains_north
    #The answer is
    result = trains_south
    return result

    seats_737_800 = 189

    #Total points
    total_points = 5000
    #Points from the 2018-2019 season
    points_2018 = 2000
    #Points from the 2019-2020 season
    points_2019 = 1500
    #Points from the 2020-2021 season
    points_2020 = total_points - points_2018 - points_2019

Topic: Minecraft ### Response:  Question: In Minecraft, you can have up to 1024 blocks in your inventory. 
A shovel can mine 64 blocks of dirt per use. 
A pickaxe can mine 16 blocks of dirt per use. 
How many uses of a shovel and a pickaxe would it take to mine 1024 blocks of dirt?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The inventory limit is 1024 blocks
    inventory_limit = 1024
    #A shovel can mine 64 blocks of dirt per use
    shovel_blocks_per_use = 64
    #A pickaxe can mine 16 blocks of dirt per use
    pickaxe_blocks_per_use = 16
    #The answer is
    result = (inventory_limit / shovel_blocks_per_use) + (inventory_limit / pickaxe_blocks_per_use)
    return result

Topic: cats ### Response:  Question: A cat has 30 whiskers in total. 10 whiskers are on its head, 8 whiskers are on its face, and the rest are on its body. How many whiskers are on its body?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A cat has 30 whiskers in total
    whiskers_total = 30
    #10 whiskers are on its head
    whiskers_head = 10
    #8 whiskers are on its face
    whiskers_face = 8
    #The rest are on its body
    whiskers_body = whiskers_total - whiskers_head - whiskers_face
    return whiskers_body

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: 
Alice and Bob went to the ice cream shop. Alice bought 3 scoops of ice cream and Bob bought 2 scoops of ice cream. 1 scoop of ice cream has 200 calories. How many calories did they consume?

Solution:

def solution():
    #Alice bought 3 scoops of ice cream
    alice_scoops = 3
    #Bob bought 2 scoops of ice cream
    bob_scoops = 2
    #1 scoop of ice cream has 200 calories
    calories_per_scoop = 200
    #The total calories is
    total_calories = (alice_scoops + bob_scoops) * calories_per_scoop
    return total_calories

Topic: cars ### Response:  Question: A parking lot has 200 spots. 120 of the spots are for cars and the rest are for motorcycles. If 160 spots are filled, how many more spots are left for motorcycles?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total spots
    total_spots = 200
    #Spots for cars
    spots_cars = 120
    #Spots for motorcycles
    spots_motorcycles = total_spots - spots_cars
    #The spots filled
    filled_spots = 160
    #The spots left for motorcycles are
    result = spots_motorcycles - filled_spots
    return result
Topic: Pokémon ### Response:  Question: There are 2400 Pokémon in the Kanto region. 1200 of them are in the Pokédex. 600 are in the Safari Zone. The rest are in the Viridian Forest. How many are in the Viridian Forest?
Solution:
def solution():
    #There are 2400 Pokémon in the Kanto region
    pokemon_total = 2400
    #1200 of them are in the Pokédex
    pokemon_pokedex = 1200
    #600 are in the Safari Zone
    pokemon_safari_zone = 600
    #The rest are in the Viridian Forest. The answer is
    pokemon_viridian_forest = pokemon_total - pokemon_pokedex - pokemon_safari_zone
    return pokemon_viridian_forest

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question:
Julia has 12 sticks of string cheese. She has 5 more sticks of string cheese than Lily. If they combine their string cheese, how many sticks do they have in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Julia has 12 sticks of string cheese
    julia_string_cheese = 12
    #She has 5 more sticks than Lily
    lily_string_cheese = julia_string_cheese - 5
    #Total sticks of string cheese
    total = julia_string_cheese + lily_string_cheese
    return total

Topic: lacrosse ### Response:  Question: 12 players on each team in a lacrosse game. 

- 60% of the players are boys
- 40% of the players are girls

If 2 of the players on each team are goalies, how many players on each team are not goalies?

Solution:
def solution():
    #12 players on each team
    players_per_team = 12
    #2 of the players on each team are goalies
    goalies = 2
    #The rest are not goalies
    not_goalies = players_per_team - goalies
    #60% of the players are boys
    boys = 0.6 * players_per_team
    #40% of the players are girls
    girls = 0.4 * players_per_team
    #The answer is
    result = not_goalies - boys - girls
    return result

Topic: Naruto ### Response:  Question: Naruto, the protagonist of the Naruto anime, is on a mission. He has 2000 ryo (currency in the Naruto world). He spends 500 ryo on a taxi to get to the mission. He spends 1000 ryo on the mission. How much ryo does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Naruto started with 2000 ryo
    ryo_initial = 2000
    #He spent 500 ryo on a taxi
    ryo_taxi = 500
    #He spent 1000 ryo on the mission
    ryo_mission = 1000
    #The answer is
    result = ryo_initial - ryo_taxi - ryo_mission
    return result

Topic: Hello Kitty ### Response:  Question: Hello Kitty has 1000 followers on Instagram. 200 more people follow her on Instagram. 150 followers are fake accounts and 300 are bots. How many real people are following Hello Kitty?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Hello Kitty has 1000 followers on Instagram
    followers_initial = 1000
    #200 more people follow her on Instagram
    followers_added = 200
    #150 followers are fake accounts
    fake_accounts = 150
    #300 are bots
    bots = 300
    #The answer is
    result = followers_initial + followers_added - fake_accounts - bots
    return result

Topic: field hockey ### Response:  Question: 16 field hockey players on a team. 11 players are on the field. 5 players are on the bench. How many players are not on the field?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of players
    total_players = 16
    #Number of players on the field
    players_on_field = 11
    #Number of players on the bench
    players_on_bench = 5
    #The answer is
    result = total_players - players_on_field
    return result

Topic: Pokémon ### Response:  Question: Pikachu has 100 lightning bolts. He uses 20 to fight Pikachu Rock, 30 to fight Pikachu Beach, and 40 to fight Pikachu Mountain. How many lightning bolts does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Pikachu started with 100 lightning bolts
    lightning_bolts_initial = 100
    #He used 20 to fight Pikachu Rock, 30 to fight Pikachu Beach, and 40 to fight Pikachu Mountain
    lightning_bolts_used = 20 + 30 + 40
    #The answer is
    result = lightning_bolts_initial - lightning_bolts_used
    return result

Topic: Iron Man ### Response:  Question: Iron Man is a superhero. He can fly at a speed of 2000 mph. If he flies from New York to Los Angeles, which is 2700 miles, how long does it take him to get to the city?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man's speed
    speed = 2000
    #Distance from New York to Los Angeles
    distance = 2700
    #The answer is
    result = distance / speed
    return result

Topic: soccer ### Response:  Question: There are 25 players on the soccer field. 15 of the players are on the 1st team. 5 of the players are on the 2nd team. 3 of the players are the referees. How many players are not referees?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of players
    total_players = 25
    #Number of 1st team players
    first_team = 15
    #Number of 2nd team players
    second_team = 5
    #Number of referees
    referees = 3
    #The answer is
    result = total_players - referees
    return result

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: 
Solution:
def solution():
    #Ice cream costs $3 a scoop
    cost_per_scoop = 3
    #Sarah has $50
    sarah_money = 50
    #She wants to buy 15 scoops
    scoops_wanted = 15
    #Each time she buys a scoop, she gets $1.25 in change.
    change_per_scoop = 1.25
    total_cost = cost_per_scoop * scoops_wanted
    total_change = change_per_scoop * scoops_wanted
    remaining_money = sarah_money - total_cost + total_change
    return remaining_money

    #Bowser is on the 10th floor
    floor_bowser = 10

Topic: field hockey ### Response:  Question: There were 480 field hockey sticks in the storage room.  They removed 40 sticks that were too short, and 30 sticks that were too long.  They added 60 sticks that were the perfect length.  How many sticks are now in the storage room? 
Solution:
def solution():
    #There were 480 sticks in the storage room
    sticks_initial = 480
    #They removed 40 sticks that were too short
    sticks_removed_short = 40
    #30 sticks that were too long
    sticks_removed_long = 30
    #60 sticks that were the perfect length. The answer is
    sticks_added = 60
    result = sticks_initial - sticks_removed_short - sticks_removed_long + sticks_added
    return result

Topic: dogs ### Response:  Question: 10 dogs have 20 toys each. 20 more dogs come and bring their toys with them. Each dog has 3 toys. How many toys are there in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #10 dogs have 20 toys each
    toys_per_dog = 20
    #20 more dogs come and bring their toys with them
    more_dogs = 20
    #Each dog has 3 toys
    toys_per_dog = 3
    #The answer is
    total_toys = (toys_per_dog * 10) + (toys_per_dog * more_dogs)
    return total_toys

Topic: LeBron James ### Response:  Question: LeBron James has scored 35,000 points in his career. He has 12,000 more points than the next best scorer. How many points has the next best scorer scored?
Solution:
def solution():
    #LeBron James has scored 35,000 points in his career
    lebron_points = 35000
    #He has 12,000 more points than the next best scorer
    next_best_points = lebron_points - 12000
    return next_best_points
Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: In the freezer,  John has 10 pints of vanilla ice cream and 20 pints of chocolate ice cream. He's having a party and he's afraid that he won't have enough ice cream, so he goes to the store to buy more. He buys 10 more pints of vanilla ice cream and 15 more pints of chocolate ice cream.  How many pints of ice cream does he have now?
Solution:
def solution():
    #John started with 10 pints of vanilla and 20 pints of chocolate
    vanilla_initial = 10
    chocolate_initial = 20
    #He bought 10 more vanilla and 15 more chocolate
    vanilla_bought = 10
    chocolate_bought = 15
    #The answer is
    result = vanilla_initial + vanilla_bought + chocolate_initial + chocolate_bought
    return result

Solution:

    #Black Panther is a king. He has 20 wives
    wives = 20
    #Each wife has 10 kids
    kids_per_wife = 10
    #The answer is
    result = wives * kids_per_wife
    return result

Topic: cats ### Response:  Question: 

Alice has 18 cats. 5 of them are black, 4 of them are white, and the rest are a mixture of colors. 

How many of them are a mixture of colors?

Solution:

def solution():

    #Total cats

    total_cats = 18

    #Black cats

    black_cats = 5

    #White cats

    white_cats = 4

    #The rest are a mixture of colors

    mixed_cats = total_cats - black_cats - white_cats

    #The answer is

    result = mixed_cats

    return result

Topic: lacrosse ### Response:  Question: A high school lacrosse team has 27 players, including 3 goalies. 10 of the players are left-handed. 5 of the left-handed players and 2 right-handed players are goalies. How many left-handed players are not goalies?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total players
    total_players = 27
    #Goalies
    goalies = 3
    #Left-handed players
    left_handed_players = 10
    #Left-handed goalies
    left_handed_goalies = 5
    #Right-handed goalies
    right_handed_goalies = 2
    #Left-handed players who are not goalies is
    left_handed_non_goalies = left_handed_players - left_handed_goalies
    return left_handed_non_goalies
Topic: Serena Williams ### Response:  Question: Serena Williams has 24 Wimbledon trophies. She has 13 more than 2 times the number of Australian Open trophies. How many Australian Open trophies does she have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena has 24 Wimbledon trophies
    wimbledon_trophies = 24
    #She has 13 more than 2 times the number of Australian Open trophies
    australian_open_trophies = (2 * wimbledon_trophies) - 13
    #The answer is
    result = australian_open_trophies
    return result

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response:  Question: T-Rex is 30 feet long, Velociraptor is 6.5 feet long, and Pterodactyl is 10.5 feet long. If a T-Rex has 5 Velociraptors and 2 Pterodactyls, how long is the T-Rex and its entourage?
Solution:
def solution():
    #T-Rex is 30 feet long
    t_rex_length = 30
    #Velociraptor is 6.5 feet long
    velociraptor_length = 6.5
    #Pterodactyl is 10.5 feet long
    pterodactyl_length = 10.5
    #If a T-Rex has 5 Velociraptors and 2 Pterodactyls, 
    velociraptors = 5
    pterodactyls = 2
    #The answer is
    result = t_rex_length + (velociraptor_length * velociraptors) + (pterodactyl_length * pterodactyls)
    return result

Topic: Minecraft ### Response:  Question: In Minecraft, a player has 100 health points. Each time they are hit, they lose 5 health points. If they are hit 20 times, how many health points do they have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A player has 100 health points
    health_points = 100
    #Each time they are hit, they lose 5 health points
    health_lost_per_hit = 5
    #If they are hit 20 times
    hits = 20
    #The answer is
    result = health_points - health_lost_per_hit * hits
    return result
Topic: basketball ### Response:  Question: The Los Angeles Lakers have 5 starting players. 3 of the players are 25 years old. 1 of the players is 27 years old. 1 of the players is 23 years old. What is the average age of the 5 players?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The total number of players
    total_players = 5
    #3 of the players are 25 years old
    players_25 = 3
    #1 of the players is 27 years old
    players_27 = 1
    #1 of the players is 23 years old
    players_23 = 1
    #The total age is
    total_age = (players_25 * 25) + (players_27 * 27) + (players_23 * 23)
    #The answer is
    result = total_age / total_players
    return result

Topic: football ### Response:  Question: 

def solution():
    #Total number of teams
    total_teams = 32
    #Number of teams in each division
    divisions = 4
    #Number of games each team plays in their division
    division_games = 6
    #Number of games each team plays in the conference
    conference_games = 8
    #Number of games each team plays in the league
    league_games = 16
    #Total number of games each team plays
    total_games = divisions * division_games + conference_games + league_games
    return total_games

Topic: Super Mario ### Response:  Question: Super Mario has 3 hammers. He used 2 hammers to break a Brick Block, and 1 hammer to break a Koopa. How many hammers does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Super Mario started with 3 hammers
    hammers_initial = 3
    #He used 2 hammers to break a Brick Block
    hammers_brick_block = 2
    #And 1 hammer to break a Koopa
    hammers_koopa = 1
    #The answer is
    result = hammers_initial - hammers_brick_block - hammers_koopa
    return result

    #He has 500 more points than the next best scorer
    next_best_scorer_points = mahomes_points - 500

Topic: Spiderman ### Response:  Question: Spiderman can shoot 20 webs per minute. He shoots 20 webs to capture a criminal. He then shoots 30 webs to save a kitten. How many more webs does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Spiderman can shoot 20 webs per minute
    webs_per_minute = 20
    #He shoots 20 webs to capture a criminal
    webs_criminal = 20
    #He then shoots 30 webs to save a kitten
    webs_kitten = 30
    #The answer is
    result = webs_per_minute - (webs_criminal + webs_kitten)
    return result

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of Power Rangers
    total_rangers = 5
    #Number of Red Rangers
    red_rangers = 2
    #Number of Blue Rangers
    blue_rangers = 2
    #Number of Yellow Rangers
    yellow_ranger = 1
    #Number of Green Rangers
    green_ranger = 1
    #Number of Rangers who are not Red
    non_red_rangers = total_rangers - red_rangers
    #The answer is
    result = non_red_rangers
    return result

Topic: cookies ### Response:  Question: 
If 50 Chocolate Chip cookies are baked in 25 minutes, how many cookies can be baked in 10 minutes? 

Solution:
def solution():
    #25 minutes is the time required for baking 50 cookies
    time_for_50_cookies = 25
    #10 minutes is the new time
    new_time = 10
    #50 cookies are the cookies baked in 25 minutes
    cookies_in_25_minutes = 50
    #The number of cookies that can be baked in 10 minutes is
    result = (cookies_in_25_minutes / time_for_50_cookies) * new_time
    return result

Topic: cars ### Response: 2020 was a bad year for the Tesla car company. They sold 2500 fewer cars than in 2009. 2011 was an even worse year. They sold 2500 more cars than in 2020. How many cars did they sell in 2020 and 2011?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Tesla sold 2500 fewer cars in 2020 than in 2009
    cars_2020 = 2500 - 2500
    #They sold 2500 more in 2011 than in 2020
    cars_2011 = cars_2020 + 2500
    #The answer is
    result = cars_2020 + cars_2011
    return result

Topic: soccer ### Response:  Question: The soccer team has 2000 supporters. 200 of them are from the United States, 300 are from the United Kingdom, and 400 are from Germany. The rest of the supporters are from other countries. How many supporters are from other countries?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total supporters
    total_supporters = 2000
    #Supporters from the United States
    supporters_us = 200
    #Supporters from the United Kingdom
    supporters_uk = 300
    #Supporters from Germany
    supporters_de = 400
    #The rest are from other countries. The answer is
    supporters_other = total_supporters - supporters_us - supporters_uk - supporters_de
    return supporters_other

Topic: Wonder Woman ### Response:  Wonder Woman can lasso 10 criminals at a time. 15 of her friends are also lassoing criminals. How many criminals have they lassoed so far?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Wonder Woman can lasso 10 criminals at a time
    wonder_woman_lasso = 10
    #15 of her friends are also lassoing criminals
    friends_lasso = 15
    #The total number of criminals they have lassoed is
    result = (wonder_woman_lasso + friends_lasso) * 10
    return result
Topic: Superman ### Response:  Question: Superman can punch 200 times per second. How many punches can he throw in 15 minutes? (15 minutes is 900 seconds.)
Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman punches 200 times per second
    punches_per_second = 200
    #15 minutes is 900 seconds
    seconds = 15 * 60
    #The answer is
    result = punches_per_second * seconds
    return result

Topic: Fortnite ### Response:  Question: 100 Fortnite players are in a match. 10 of them are eliminated. 20 more are eliminated. 30 of the players are left. How many Fortnite players are still in the match?
Solution:
def solution():
    #There were 100 players
    players_initial = 100
    #10 of them were eliminated
    eliminations_1 = 10
    #20 more were eliminated
    eliminations_2 = 20
    #30 of the players were left
    players_left = 30
    #The answer is
    result = players_initial - eliminations_1 - eliminations_2 + players_left
    return result
Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response:  Question: Captain Marvel can punch 1000 times a minute. 45 minutes ago, she punched for 30 minutes. How many punches does she have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain Marvel can punch 1000 times a minute
    punches_per_minute = 1000
    #45 minutes ago, she punched for 30 minutes
    punches_45_minutes_ago = punches_per_minute * 30
    #The answer is
    result = punches_per_minute * 45 - punches_45_minutes_ago
    return result

Topic: cars ### Response:  Question: 20 cars are in a parking lot. 10 more cars arrive. 3 of the cars in the parking lot leave. How many cars are in the parking lot now?
Solution:
def solution():
    #20 cars are in a parking lot
    cars_initial = 20
    #10 more cars arrive
    cars_arrive = 10
    #3 of the cars in the parking lot leave
    cars_leave = 3
    #The answer is
    result = cars_initial + cars_arrive - cars_leave
    return result

Topic: swimming ### Response:  Question: 5 turtles are in a swimming pool. 3 of them are 2 years old. 1 of them is 3 years old. 1 of them is 1 year old. What is the average age of the turtles in years?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total turtles
    turtles = 5
    #2-year-old turtles
    turtles_2 = 3
    #3-year-old turtle
    turtle_3 = 1
    #1-year-old turtle
    turtle_1 = 1
    #Total age
    total_age = (turtles_2 * 2) + (turtle_3 * 3) + (turtle_1 * 1)
    #Average age
    average_age = total_age / turtles
    return average_age

    #The answer is

    return result

Topic: candy ### Response:  Question: 
Alice and Bob are playing a game with candy. 

Alice has 25 

Bob has 15 

In each round, each player can 

   Alice 

   Bob 

They play until everyone 

The first player to run out of candy 

The winner of the game is 

Solution: def solution():

    # Number of candies each player has
    alice_candies = 25
    bob_candies = 15

    # They each use 2 candies per round
    candies_per_round = 2

    # Calculate how many rounds they play
    rounds = min(alice_candies // candies_per_round, bob_candies // candies_per_round)

    # If Alice runs out of candies first
    if alice_candies - rounds * candies_per_round == 0:
        winner = "Alice"
    # If Bob runs out of candies first
    elif bob_candies - rounds * candies_per_round == 0:
        winner = "Bob"
    # If they both run out of candies at the same time
    else:
        winner = "It's a tie"

    # The answer is
    result = winner
    return result

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response:  Question: Captain Marvel has 3255 vibranium shards. 2000 of the shards are in her vault, and the rest are in her armory. How many shards are in her armory?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain Marvel has 3255 vibranium shards
    vibranium_shards_total = 3255
    #2000 of the shards are in her vault
    shards_vault = 2000
    #The rest are in her armory
    shards_armory = vibranium_shards_total - shards_vault
    return shards_armory

Topic: ice cream ### Response: 1. You have 300 pennies. You spend 100 pennies to buy a scoop of ice cream. 2. The scoop of ice cream has 50 calories. 3. A single calorie is 1000 pennies. 4. You want to buy a second scoop of ice cream. How many pennies do you have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #We started with 300 pennies
    pennies_initial = 300
    #We spent 100 pennies on a scoop of ice cream
    pennies_spent = 100
    #A scoop of ice cream is 50 calories
    calories_per_scoop = 50
    #1 calorie is 1000 pennies
    pennies_per_calorie = 1000
    #We want to buy a second scoop of ice cream
    #The second scoop will be
    scoop_2 = calories_per_scoop
    #We have
    pennies_left = pennies_initial - pennies_spent - scoop_2 * pennies_per_calorie
    #The answer is
    result = pennies_left
    return result

    #They have 15 scoops of vanilla
    ice_cream_scoops_vanilla = 15
    #They have 10 scoops of strawberry
    ice_cream_scoops_strawberry = 10

    return result

Topic: Patrick Mahomes ### Response:  Patrick Mahomes, the star quarterback of the Kansas City Chiefs, is the most prolific passer in the history of the league. He has 5000 career passing yards. 

John Elway, the legendary quarterback of the Denver Broncos, has 500 fewer career passing yards than Patrick Mahomes. 

How many career passing yards do John Elway and Patrick Mahomes have combined?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Patrick Mahomes has 5000 career passing yards
    mahomes_passing_yards = 5000
    #John Elway has 500 fewer
    elway_passing_yards = mahomes_passing_yards - 500
    #The answer is
    result = mahomes_passing_yards + elway_passing_yards
    return result

Topic: trains ### Response: 10 trains left the station. 
Each train has 3 cars. 
There are 2 people in each car. 
How many people are on the trains?
Solution:
def solution():
    #10 trains left the station
    trains = 10
    #Each train has 3 cars
    cars_per_train = 3
    #There are 2 people in each car
    people_per_car = 2
    #The answer is
    result = trains * cars_per_train * people_per_car
    return result

Topic: unicorns ### Response:  Question: UniWorld is home to 200 unicorns. 40% of the unicorns are pink, 30% are blue, and 30% are yellow. 
How many unicorns are not one of these colors?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total unicorns
    total_unicorns = 200
    #40% of the unicorns are pink
    pink_unicorns = total_unicorns * 0.40
    #30% of the unicorns are blue
    blue_unicorns = total_unicorns * 0.30
    #30% of the unicorns are yellow
    yellow_unicorns = total_unicorns * 0.30
    #The answer is
    result = total_unicorns - pink_unicorns - blue_unicorns - yellow_unicorns
    return result

    power_gems_red_blue_yellow = 8 * 3
    #Pink and Green Power Ranger each have 2 Power Gems
    power_gems_pink_green = 2 * 2
    #The answer is

    return result

Solution:
def solution():
    #Harry Potter started with 300 galleons
    galleons_initial = 300
    #He bought 100 more galleons
    galleons_bought = 100
    #He lent 200 galleons to Ron
    galleons_lent_ron = 200
    #He lent 200 more galleons to Hermione
    galleons_lent_hermione = 200
    #The answer is
    result = galleons_initial + galleons_bought - galleons_lent_ron - galleons_lent_hermione
    return result

Topic: soccer ### Response:  Question: 12 soccer players on a team. 5 of them are forwards, 4 of them are midfielders, and the rest are defenders. 2 of the defenders are goalies. How many soccer players are not goalies?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of players
    total_players = 12
    #Number of forwards
    forwards = 5
    #Number of midfielders
    midfielders = 4
    #Number of defenders
    defenders = total_players - forwards - midfielders
    #Number of goalies
    goalies = 2
    #The answer is
    result = defenders - goalies
    return result

Topic: field hockey ### Response:  QUESTION:  In field hockey, a team has 11 players on the field at a time. 1 of the players is the goalie. 3 of the players are defenders. 2 of the players are forward. 5 of the players are midfielders. How many more midfielders than forwards are there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #total players on the field
    total_players = 11
    #number of goalies
    goalies = 1
    #number of defenders
    defenders = 3
    #number of forwards
    forwards = 2
    #number of midfielders
    midfielders = 5
    #number of midfielders more than forwards
    result = midfielders - forwards
    return result

Topic: dogs ### Response:  Question: 20 of the dogs in the park are Poodles. 2 of the Poodles are white. 4 of the dogs are Dachshunds.  Half of the Dachshunds are tan. How many dogs in the park are not Poodles or Dachshunds?
Solution:
def solution():
    #20 of the dogs in the park are Poodles
    poodles = 20
    #2 of the Poodles are white
    poodles_white = 2
    #4 of the dogs are Dachshunds
    dachshunds = 4
    #Half of the Dachshunds are tan
    dachshunds_tan = dachshunds / 2
    #The answer is
    result = (poodles + poodles_white + dachshunds + dachshunds_tan)
    return result

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: 200 scoops of ice cream were served. 50 of them were chocolate, 50 of them were vanilla, and the rest were strawberry. How many of them were strawberry?
Solution:
def solution():
    #200 scoops of ice cream were served
    scoops_total = 200
    #50 of them were chocolate
    scoops_chocolate = 50
    #50 of them were vanilla
    scoops_vanilla = 50
    #The rest were strawberry. The answer is
    scoops_strawberry = scoops_total - scoops_chocolate - scoops_vanilla
    return scoops_strawberry

2. Spider-Man can shoot 10 webs in 15 seconds. 20 villains are after him. They are 1000 feet away. If each web can reach 250 feet, how many seconds will Spider-Man take to web all the villains?
Solution:

def solution():
    #Spider-Man can shoot 10 webs in 15 seconds
    webs_per_minute = 10 / 15
    #20 villains are after him
    villains = 20
    #They are 1000 feet away
    distance = 1000
    #Each web can reach 250 feet
    web_range = 250
    #The answer is
    result = (distance / web_range) * (1 / webs_per_minute)
    return result

Topic: pizza ### Response:  Question: It takes 6 slices of pizza to fill a large box. 10 of these large boxes will fill a delivery van. A pizza has 16 slices. How many pizzas does it take to fill the delivery van?
Solution:
def solution():
    #1 large box
    slices_per_box = 6
    #10 large boxes
    boxes_per_van = 10
    #1 pizza
    slices_per_pizza = 16
    #The answer is
    result = (slices_per_box * boxes_per_van) / slices_per_pizza
    return result
Topic: football ### Response:  Question: A football team has 100 players. 

40 of the players are on the offense. 

35 of the players are on the defense. 

The rest of the players are on special teams. 

How many players are on special teams?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A football team has 100 players
    players_total = 100
    #40 of the players are on the offense
    players_offense = 40
    #35 of the players are on the defense
    players_defense = 35
    #The answer is
    players_special_teams = players_total - players_offense - players_defense
    return players_special_teams

Topic: Minecraft ### Response:  Question: 
Alice has 1000 minerals. She has 100 more minerals than Bob. 

Charlie has 2000 minerals. 

Lily has 200 more minerals than Charlie. 

How many minerals do Alice, Bob, Charlie, and Lily have in total?
Solution: 
def solution():
    #Alice has 1000 minerals
    alice_minerals = 1000
    #She has 100 more minerals than Bob
    bob_minerals = alice_minerals - 100
    #Charlie has 2000 minerals
    charlie_minerals = 2000
    #Lily has 200 more minerals than Charlie
    lily_minerals = charlie_minerals + 200
    #The total minerals is
    total_minerals = alice_minerals + bob_minerals + charlie_minerals + lily_minerals
    return total_minerals
Topic: volleyball ### Response:  Volleyball Word Problem Solution
def volleyball_word_problem():

    # 12 teams participated in the volleyball tournament

    teams = 12

    # 3 of the teams were from the United States

    us_teams = 3

    # 2 of the teams were from Canada

    canada_teams = 2

    # 5 of the teams were from Mexico

    mexico_teams = 5

    # Calculate the number of teams from other countries

    other_countries_teams = teams - us_teams - canada_teams - mexico_teams

    # The answer is

    result = us_teams + canada_teams + mexico_teams + other_countries_teams

    return result

```
def solution():
    #There were 50 T-Rexes in the park
    t_rex = 50
    #20 of the T-Rexes were male
    t_rex_male = 20
    #30 of the T-Rexes were female
    t_rex_female = 30
    #The answer is
    result = (t_rex_male * 4) + (t_rex_female * 3)
    return result
```

Topic: basketball ### Response:  Question: LeBron James is a basketball superstar. He is 6'9" tall. He can jump 48" high. He is 3" taller than the average person who can jump 36" high. How many inches higher can LeBron James jump than the average person?
Solution:
def solution():
    #LeBron is 6'9" tall, which is 81"
    lebron_height = 81
    #He can jump 48" high
    lebron_jump = 48
    #The average person who is 3" shorter than LeBron can jump 36" high
    average_height = lebron_height - 3
    average_jump = 36
    #The answer is
    result = lebron_jump - average_jump
    return result

Topic: Hello Kitty ### Response:  Question: 

Hello Kitty has 12 pink pencils.  She has 20 more yellow pencils.  She has 50% more black pencils than pink and yellow pencils combined.  How many pencils does Hello Kitty have in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Hello Kitty has 12 pink pencils
    pink_pencils = 12
    #She has 20 more yellow pencils
    yellow_pencils = 20
    #She has 50% more black pencils than pink and yellow pencils combined
    black_pencils = (pink_pencils + yellow_pencils) * 1.5
    #The answer is
    result = pink_pencils + yellow_pencils + black_pencils
    return result

Topic: planes ### Response:  Question: 200 planes at an airport are to be towed by a tractor. 50 of the planes are too big for the tractor, so they will be towed by a larger vehicle. 30 of the planes are missing a wheel, so they will need to be towed slowly. 20 of the planes are in the airport's hanger and will need to be towed out. How many planes will be towed by the tractor?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of planes
    total_planes = 200
    #50 of the planes are too big for the tractor
    too_big_for_tractor = 50
    #30 of the planes are missing a wheel
    missing_wheel = 30
    #20 of the planes are in the airport's hanger
    hanger_planes = 20
    #The rest of the planes will be towed by the tractor
    tractor_planes = total_planes - (too_big_for_tractor + missing_wheel + hanger_planes)
    return tractor_planes

    #He has 500 more webshots than Spiderman: Homecoming
    spiderman_homecoming_webshots = spiderman_webshots - 500
    #He has 2000 more webshots than Spiderman: Into the Spider-Verse
