Topic: pizza ### Response:  Question: 10 friends are ordering pizza. Each of them wants 3 slices. If a large pizza has 18 slices, how many pizzas do they need to order?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Number of friends
    friends = 10
    #Slices per friend
    slices_per_friend = 3
    #Total slices required
    total_slices_required = friends * slices_per_friend
    #Size of pizza
    pizza_slices = 18
    #Number of pizzas required
    pizzas_required = total_slices_required / pizza_slices
    #The answer is
    result = pizzas_required
    return result

Topic: Patrick Mahomes ### Response:  Question: Patrick Mahomes is the quarterback for the Kansas City Chiefs. He has 2000 passing yards. He has 400 more passing yards than the second best quarterback. How many passing yards does the second best quarterback have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Patrick Mahomes has 2000 passing yards
    mahomes_passing_yards = 2000
    #He has 400 more passing yards than the second best quarterback
    difference = 400
    #The second best quarterback has
    second_best_passing_yards = mahomes_passing_yards - difference
    #The answer is
    result = second_best_passing_yards
    return result

Topic: dogs ### Response:  Question: Darcy has 35 dogs. Heidi has 48 dogs. 1/4 of Heidi's dogs are the same breed as 1/2 of Darcy's dogs. How many dogs do Darcy and Heidi have that are not the same breed?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Darcy has 35 dogs
    darcy_dogs = 35
    #Heidi has 48 dogs
    heidi_dogs = 48
    #1/4 of Heidi's dogs are the same breed as 1/2 of Darcy's dogs
    same_breed = ((darcy_dogs * 1/2) * 1/4) + ((heidi_dogs * 1/4) * 1/2)
    #Dogs that are not the same breed are
    not_same_breed = darcy_dogs + heidi_dogs - same_breed
    #The answer is
    result = int(not_same_breed)
    return result

    total_players = 120
    #Players on the offense
    offense_players = 40
    #Players on the defense
    defense_players = 50
    #Officials
    officials = 30
    #Players that were not officials
    non_officials = total_players - officials
    return non_officials

Topic: swimming ### Response:  "Fred has 200 square meters of swimming pool. He fills it to a depth of 2 meters. He then divides the pool into 4 equal sections. How many cubic meters are in each section?"
Solution:
def solution():
    #Fred has 200 square meters of swimming pool
    pool_area = 200
    #He fills it to a depth of 2 meters
    pool_depth = 2
    #He then divides the pool into 4 equal sections
    sections = 4
    #The volume of each section is
    result = (pool_area * pool_depth) / sections
    return result

Topic: Hello Kitty ### Response: 1. Hello Kitty has 12 toys. She bought 2 more toys at the toy store. 2. She lent 3 toys to her friend. 3. She lost 1 toy in the wash. 4. How many toys does Hello Kitty have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Hello Kitty has 12 toys
    toys_initial = 12
    #She bought 2 more toys
    toys_bought = 2
    #She lent 3 toys to her friend
    toys_lent = 3
    #She lost 1 toy in the wash
    toys_lost = 1
    #The answer is
    result = toys_initial + toys_bought - toys_lent - toys_lost
    return result

Topic: candy ### Response:  Question: 

Mickey has 1000 candies. He has 500 more candies than Minnie. 200 of the candies are pink. 1/2 of the pink candies are cherry. 1/4 of the cherry candies are strawberry. How many strawberry candies are there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Mickey has 1000 candies
    mickey_candies = 1000
    #He has 500 more candies than Minnie
    minnie_candies = mickey_candies - 500
    #200 of the candies are pink
    pink_candies = 200
    #1/2 of the pink candies are cherry
    cherry_candies = pink_candies / 2
    #1/4 of the cherry candies are strawberry
    strawberry_candies = cherry_candies / 4
    #The answer is
    result = int(strawberry_candies)
    return result
Topic: dinosaurs ### Response:  Question: T-Rex's jaw can open 4 feet wide. Velociraptor's jaw can open 1/10 as wide as T-Rex. Pteranodon's jaw can open 1/2 as wide as Velociraptor. How much wider can T-Rex's jaw open than Pteranodon's?
Solution:
def solution():
    #T-Rex's jaw can open 4 feet wide
    t_rex_jaw_width = 4
    #Velociraptor's jaw can open 1/10 as wide as T-Rex
    velociraptor_jaw_width = t_rex_jaw_width / 10
    #Pteranodon's jaw can open 1/2 as wide as Velociraptor
    pteranodon_jaw_width = velociraptor_jaw_width / 2
    #The difference in width between T-Rex and Pteranodon's jaws is
    result = t_rex_jaw_width - pteranodon_jaw_width
    return result

Topic: Power Rangers ### Response:  Question: 

Red, Blue, Yellow, and Pink Power Rangers have to buy new helmets. Red Power Ranger's helmet costs $30, Blue Power Ranger's helmet costs $25, Yellow Power Ranger's helmet costs $22, and Pink Power Ranger's helmet costs $28. 

If they have $100 to spend, how much money will be left after they buy each of them a helmet?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Each of them costs
    red_helmet_cost = 30
    blue_helmet_cost = 25
    yellow_helmet_cost = 22
    pink_helmet_cost = 28
    #They have
    total_money = 100

    #The answer is
    result = total_money - (red_helmet_cost + blue_helmet_cost + yellow_helmet_cost + pink_helmet_cost)
    return result
Topic: Fortnite ### Response:  Question: There were 100 people in a Fortnite match. 20 of them were eliminated in the first 5 minutes. 40 more were eliminated in the next 5 minutes. 50 were left at the end of the match. How many people were eliminated altogether?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total people in the match
    total_people = 100
    #People eliminated in the first 5 minutes
    eliminated_1 = 20
    #People eliminated in the next 5 minutes
    eliminated_2 = 40
    #People left at the end of the match
    remaining = 50
    #The answer is
    result = total_people - eliminated_1 - eliminated_2 - remaining
    return result

Topic: volleyball ### Response:  Question: A volleyball team is 6 people. In the first set, they won 12 points. In the second set, they won 15 points. In the third set, they won 11 points. How many points did they win in total?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The volleyball team is 6 people
    team_size = 6
    #In the first set, they won 12 points
    set1_won = 12
    #In the second set, they won 15 points
    set2_won = 15
    #In the third set, they won 11 points
    set3_won = 11
    #The total points they won is
    result = team_size * (set1_won + set2_won + set3_won)
    return result
Topic: soccer ### Response: 11 players on each team, 2 periods of 25 minutes each, 1 halftime, 1 final score question. Solution:
def solution():
    #Each team has 11 players
    players_per_team = 11
    #2 periods of 25 minutes each
    period_length = 2 * 25
    #1 halftime
    halftime_length = 15
    #1 final score question
    final_score_question = 1
    #The total time in minutes is
    total_time = period_length * 2 + halftime_length + final_score_question
    return total_time

Topic: Wonder Woman ### Response:  Question: 1000000000 golden apples fell from the heavens, and 1000000000 more appeared in the forest. 

- 2000000000 golden apples were eaten by 10000000 humans.
- 2000000000 golden apples were eaten by 1000000000 monkeys.
- 2000000000 golden apples were eaten by 1000000000 dinosaurs.
- 2000000000 golden apples were eaten by 1000000000 elephants.

How many golden apples are left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The total number of golden apples initially
    total_apples = 1000000000 + 1000000000
    #The number of golden apples eaten by each type of being
    humans = 10000000
    monkeys = 1000000000
    dinosaurs = 1000000000
    elephants = 1000000000
    #The total number of golden apples eaten
    total_eaten = humans + monkeys + dinosaurs + elephants
    #The answer is
    result = total_apples - total_eaten
    return result

Topic: Serena Williams ### Response:  Question: Serena Williams is the best tennis player in the world. She has 100 Grand Slam titles. 25 of them are in singles, 30 are in doubles, and the rest are in mixed doubles. How many Grand Slam titles does she have in mixed doubles?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total Grand Slam titles
    total_titles = 100
    #Single titles
    single_titles = 25
    #Doubles titles
    doubles_titles = 30
    #Mixed doubles titles is
    mixed_doubles_titles = total_titles - single_titles - doubles_titles
    return mixed_doubles_titles

Topic: dinosaurs ### Response:  Question: In the movie Jurassic Park, it cost $25,000 to transport each dinosaur. It cost $15,000 to keep each dinosaur alive. They transported 25 dinosaurs and had 150 in the park. How much did it cost to run the park?
Solution:
def solution():
    #It cost $25,000 to transport each dinosaur
    transport_cost = 25000
    #It cost $15,000 to keep each dinosaur alive
    maintenance_cost = 15000
    #They transported 25 dinosaurs
    transported_dinosaurs = 25
    #They had 150 in the park
    park_dinosaurs = 150
    #The total cost is
    result = (transport_cost * transported_dinosaurs) + (maintenance_cost * park_dinosaurs)
    return result

Topic: trains ### Response:  Question: At the train station, a train leaves every 10 minutes. Each train has 3 cars. If 2 trains have left the station, and the next train leaves in 5 minutes, how many train cars are at the station?
Solution:
def solution():
    #The next train leaves in 5 minutes
    minutes_to_next_train = 5
    #Each train has 3 cars
    cars_per_train = 3
    #2 trains have left the station
    trains_left = 2
    #The answer is
    result = trains_left * cars_per_train + (minutes_to_next_train // 10)
    return result

Topic: Power Rangers ### Response:  Question: Mighty Morphin Power Rangers have 10 Rangers. They have to split up to 5 to 2 different locations. 2 Rangers each go to 2 different locations. 1 Ranger goes to 1 different location. How many Rangers are at each location?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of Power Rangers
    total_rangers = 10
    #They split up
    rangers_split = total_rangers // 5
    #2 Rangers each go to 2 different locations
    rangers_2_locations = 2 * 2
    #1 Ranger goes to 1 different location
    rangers_1_location = 1
    #The answer is
    result = (rangers_split, rangers_2_locations, rangers_1_location)
    return result

Topic: Patrick Mahomes ### Response:  Question: Patrick Mahomes has 200 passing yards. He passes for 2 touchdowns and 1 interception. How many net yards does he have?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Patrick Mahomes started with 200 passing yards
    passing_yards_initial = 200
    #He passed for 2 touchdowns
    touchdowns = 2
    #He had 1 interception
    interceptions = 1
    #A touchdown is worth 10 yards, and an interception is worth -10 yards
    touchdown_yards = touchdowns * 10
    interception_yards = interceptions * -10
    #The total net yards is
    result = passing_yards_initial + touchdown_yards + interception_yards
    return result

    ron_intelligence = 150000
    #Hermione is 2.5 times smarter than Ron
    hermione_smarter = 2.5
    #Hermione's intelligence is
    hermione_intelligence = ron_intelligence * hermione_smarter
    return hermione_intelligence

Topic: Power Rangers ### Response:  Question: 5 Power Rangers are in a fight with 20 Putties. 2 of the Putties are in the sewer, and the rest are on the street. 1 of the Power Rangers is in the sewer, and the rest are on the street. How many more Putties than Power Rangers are on the street?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of Power Rangers
    total_power_rangers = 5
    #Total number of Putties
    total_putties = 20
    #Number of Putties in the sewer
    putties_in_sewer = 2
    #Number of Power Rangers in the sewer
    power_rangers_in_sewer = 1
    #Number of Putties on the street
    putties_on_street = total_putties - putties_in_sewer
    #Number of Power Rangers on the street
    power_rangers_on_street = total_power_rangers - power_rangers_in_sewer
    #The answer is
    result = putties_on_street - power_rangers_on_street

Topic: pizza ### Response:  Question: 

Pizzas have 8 slices. 

A restaurant has 20 pizzas. 

Their pizza slicer is broken so they can only slice 6 slices per pizza. 

How many slices are they missing?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Pizzas have 8 slices
    slices_per_pizza = 8
    #A restaurant has 20 pizzas
    pizzas = 20
    #Their pizza slicer is broken so they can only slice 6 slices per pizza
    slices_per_pizza_after = 6
    #The answer is
    result = (slices_per_pizza - slices_per_pizza_after) * pizzas
    return result

Topic: cheer leading ### Response:  Question: 16 cheerleaders are in a pyramid. 4 more cheerleaders are added to the top. How many cheerleaders are now in the pyramid?
Solution:
def solution():
    #16 cheerleaders are in a pyramid
    cheerleaders_initial = 16
    #4 more cheerleaders are added to the top
    cheerleaders_added = 4
    #The answer is
    result = cheerleaders_initial + cheerleaders_added
    return result
Given a building with 20 floors, each floor of which has 5 rooms, how many rooms are in the building?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Total floors in the building
    floors = 20
    #Total rooms per floor
    rooms_per_floor = 5
    #The answer is
    result = floors * rooms_per_floor
    return result

Topic: Iron Man ### Response:  Question: Iron Man has 1000 armor suits. He has to pay 500 for each one. How much does he have to pay for 200 more armor suits?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Iron Man has 1000 armor suits
    armor_suits_initial = 1000
    #He has to pay 500 for each one
    cost_per_armor_suit = 500
    #He has to pay for 200 more armor suits
    armor_suits_to_pay_for = 200
    #The answer is
    result = armor_suits_to_pay_for * cost_per_armor_suit
    return result

Topic: Black Panther ### Response:  Question: Black Panther has 5000 vibranium spears. He uses 2000 vibranium spears to fight the Jabari Tribe, 1000 vibranium spears to fight the Wakandan Army, and 500 vibranium spears to fight the Dora Milaje. How many vibranium spears does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Black Panther started with 5000 vibranium spears
    vibranium_spears_initial = 5000
    #He used 2000 to fight the Jabari Tribe
    vibranium_spears_jabari = 2000
    #1000 to fight the Wakandan Army
    vibranium_spears_wakandan = 1000
    #And 500 to fight the Dora Milaje
    vibranium_spears_dora = 500
    #The answer is
    result = vibranium_spears_initial - vibranium_spears_jabari - vibranium_spears_wakandan - vibranium_spears_dora
    return result

Topic: Super Mario ### Response:  Question:  A Toad is 25 coins.  A Koopa is 50 coins.  If 100 Toads are 3000 coins, how many Koopas are there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A Toad is 25 coins
    toad_coins = 25
    #100 Toads are 3000 coins
    toads = 100
    #3000 coins is
    toad_coins_total = 3000
    #A Koopa is 50 coins
    koopa_coins = 50
    #The answer is
    koopas = toad_coins_total / (toad_coins * toads)
    return koopas

Topic: Batman ### Response:  Question: Batman has 300 gadgets. 

He used 50 gadgets to fight the Penguin and 20 gadgets to fight the Riddler. 

He used 30 gadgets to fight the Joker and 70 gadgets to fight the rest of the villains. 

How many gadgets does he have left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Batman started with 300 gadgets
    gadgets_initial = 300
    #He used 50 gadgets to fight the Penguin
    gadgets_penguin = 50
    #20 gadgets to fight the Riddler
    gadgets_riddler = 20
    #30 gadgets to fight the Joker
    gadgets_joker = 30
    #70 gadgets to fight the rest of the villains
    gadgets_rest = 70
    #The answer is
    result = gadgets_initial - gadgets_penguin - gadgets_riddler - gadgets_joker - gadgets_rest
    return result

Topic: Superman ### Response:  Question: Superman flies 2000 miles in 20 minutes. How fast is he flying? (in miles per minute)
Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman flies 2000 miles in 20 minutes
    miles_flown = 2000
    minutes_flown = 20
    #The answer is
    result = miles_flown / minutes_flown
    return result

Topic: Ninja Turtles ### Response: 4 turtles, 3 pizzas, 2 toppings per pizza, 1 slice per topping = 12 slices of pizza.
def solution():
    #Number of turtles
    turtles = 4
    #Number of pizzas
    pizzas = 3
    #Number of toppings per pizza
    toppings = 2
    #Number of slices per topping
    slices = 1
    #The answer is
    result = turtles * pizzas * toppings * slices
    return result

Topic: trains ### Response:  Question: 250 trains are in a train station. 50 more trains arrive. 20 trains leave. How many trains are left in the station?
Solution:
def solution():

    #250 trains are in a train station

    trains_initial = 250

    #50 more trains arrive

    trains_arrive = 50

    #20 trains leave

    trains_leave = 20

    #The answer is

    result = trains_initial + trains_arrive - trains_leave

    return result

Topic: unicorns ### Response:  Question: There are 20 unicorns in a field. 6 of them are pink, 5 of them are blue, 4 of them are green, and the rest are white. How many of them are white?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total number of unicorns
    total_unicorns = 20
    #Number of pink unicorns
    pink_unicorns = 6
    #Number of blue unicorns
    blue_unicorns = 5
    #Number of green unicorns
    green_unicorns = 4
    #The rest are white
    white_unicorns = total_unicorns - pink_unicorns - blue_unicorns - green_unicorns
    return white_unicorns
Topic: Minecraft ### Response:  Minecraft Question: In Minecraft, a player can have 36 slots in their inventory. 12 of the slots are for weapons, 10 are for armor, and the rest are for items.  Joe has 20 items. 20% of his items are in his hotbar, 30% are in his inventory, and the rest are in his off-hand. How many items are in his off-hand?
Solution:
def solution():
    #In Minecraft, a player can have 36 slots in their inventory. 12 of the slots are for weapons, 10 are for armor, and the rest are for items.
    #Joe has 20 items.
    #20% of his items are in his hotbar, 30% are in his inventory, and the rest are in his off-hand.
    #The answer is
    items_total = 36 - 12 - 10
    items_joe = 20
    items_hotbar = items_joe * 0.20
    items_inventory = items_joe * 0.30
    items_offhand = items_joe - items_hotbar - items_inventory
    result = items_offhand
    return result
Topic: Hello Kitty ### Response:  Question: Hello Kitty has 8 pink pencils, 6 green pencils, and 4 blue pencils.  She decides to sharpen all of her pencils.  How many pencils will she have left?

Solution:
def solution():
    #Hello Kitty has 8 pink pencils
    pink_pencils = 8
    #6 green pencils
    green_pencils = 6
    #4 blue pencils
    blue_pencils = 4
    #She decides to sharpen all of her pencils
    #Each pencil is reduced by half after sharpening
    pink_pencils_sharpened = pink_pencils / 2
    green_pencils_sharpened = green_pencils / 2
    blue_pencils_sharpened = blue_pencils / 2
    #The answer is
    result = pink_pencils_sharpened + green_pencils_sharpened + blue_pencils_sharpened
    return result
Topic: Ninja Turtles ### Response:  Question: 4 turtles ate 20 pizza slices. Leonardo ate 1/4 of the pizza slices. Michelangelo ate 1/2 of the pizza slices. Donatello ate 3/4 of the pizza slices.  How many pizza slices did Raphael eat?
Solution:
def solution():
    total_slices = 20
    leonardo_fraction = 1/4
    michelangelo_fraction = 1/2
    donatello_fraction = 3/4
    #Raphael ate the remaining slices
    raphael_fraction = 1 - (leonardo_fraction + michelangelo_fraction + donatello_fraction)
    #The answer is
    result = total_slices * raphael_fraction
    return result
Topic: cats ### Response:  Question: There are 9 kittens in a basket. Kiki, the kitten nurse, eats 3 kittens. Then, 2 more kittens are born. How many kittens are now in the basket?
Solution:
def solution():
    #There are 9 kittens in a basket
    kittens_initial = 9
    #Kiki, the kitten nurse, eats 3 kittens
    kittens_eaten = 3
    #Then, 2 more kittens are born
    kittens_born = 2
    #The answer is
    result = kittens_initial - kittens_eaten + kittens_born
    return result

Topic: Fortnite ### Response: 20 Fortnite players are in a game. 3 of them are eliminated in the first 5 minutes. 4 more are eliminated in the next 5 minutes. 3 of the remaining players are eliminated in the next 5 minutes. How many players are left?
Solution:
def solution():
    #20 players started the game
    players_start = 20
    #3 of them were eliminated in the first 5 minutes
    players_eliminated_first_5_minutes = 3
    #4 more were eliminated in the next 5 minutes
    players_eliminated_next_5_minutes = 4
    #3 of the remaining players were eliminated in the next 5 minutes
    players_eliminated_next_5_minutes_2 = 3
    #The answer is
    result = players_start - players_eliminated_first_5_minutes - players_eliminated_next_5_minutes - players_eliminated_next_5_minutes_2
    return result
Topic: Super Mario ### Response:  Question: Super Mario has 100 coins. He jumps on 20 Koopas, 30 Goombas, and 50 Piranha Plants. Each Koopa gives him 2 coins, each Goomba gives him 1 coin, and each Piranha Plant gives him 4 coins. How many coins does he have now?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Super Mario has 100 coins
    coins_initial = 100
    #He jumps on 20 Koopas
    koopas = 20
    #Each Koopa gives him 2 coins
    coins_from_koopas = koopas * 2
    #He jumps on 30 Goombas
    goombas = 30
    #Each Goomba gives him 1 coin
    coins_from_goombas = goombas * 1
    #He jumps on 50 Piranha Plants
    piranha_plants = 50
    #Each Piranha Plant gives him 4 coins
    coins_from_piranha_plants = piranha_plants * 4
    #The total coins is
    result = coins_initial + coins_from_koopas

Topic: Superman ### Response:  Question:  Superman can fly at a speed of 2000 miles per hour.  If he flies from Gotham to Metropolis, which is 500 miles, how long does it take?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Superman flies at 2000 miles per hour
    speed = 2000
    #He flies from Gotham to Metropolis, which is 500 miles
    distance = 500
    #The answer is
    result = distance / speed
    return result

Topic: Captain Marvel ### Response:  Question: Captain Marvel has 20000000000000000000 (2 quintillion) Zenn-La dollars. It costs 10000000000000000000 (1 quintillion) Zenn-La dollars to get a new outfit. 1000000000000000000 (1 trillion) Zenn-La dollars is a lot of money. How many 1 trillion Zenn-La dollar outfits can she buy?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Captain Marvel has 2 quintillion Zenn-La dollars
    marvel_money = 20000000000000000000
    #It costs 1 quintillion to get a new outfit
    outfit_cost = 10000000000000000000
    #1 trillion Zenn-La dollars is a lot of money
    one_trillion = 1000000000000000000
    #The answer is
    result = marvel_money / outfit_cost
    return result

Topic: dogs ### Response:  Question: There are 36 dogs in a dog park. 1/3 of the dogs are dachshunds, 1/2 of the dachshunds are wearing sunglasses, and 2/3 of the dogs that are not dachshunds are wearing sunglasses. How many dogs are wearing sunglasses?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Total dogs in the dog park
    total_dogs = 36
    #Dogs that are dachshunds
    dachshunds = total_dogs * (1/3)
    #Dachshunds wearing sunglasses
    dachshunds_wearing_sunglasses = dachshunds * (1/2)
    #Dogs that are not dachshunds
    non_dachshunds = total_dogs - dachshunds
    #Dogs that are not dachshunds wearing sunglasses
    non_dachshunds_wearing_sunglasses = non_dachshunds * (2/3)
    #The answer is
    result = dachshunds_wearing_sunglasses + non_dachshunds_wearing_sunglasses
    return result

Topic: Serena Williams ### Response:  Question: Serena Williams has 200 Wimbledon titles. 100 of them are in singles, 50 are in doubles, and the rest are in mixed doubles. How many Wimbledon titles does she have in mixed doubles?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Serena Williams has 200 Wimbledon titles
    total_titles = 200
    #100 of them are in singles
    singles_titles = 100
    #50 are in doubles
    doubles_titles = 50
    #The rest are in mixed doubles
    mixed_doubles_titles = total_titles - singles_titles - doubles_titles
    return mixed_doubles_titles

Topic: volleyball ### Response:  Question: 

In volleyball, each team has 6 players on the court. 

A volleyball game has 5 sets. 

Each set is won by the team that is the first to 25 points, but with no team ever leading by more than 2 points.

How many points does each team get per set on average?
Solution:
def solution():
    #Each team has 6 players
    players_per_team = 6
    #A volleyball game has 5 sets
    sets = 5
    #Each set is won by the team that is the first to 25 points, but with no team ever leading by more than 2 points.
    #So, a set can end when one team has 25 points and the other team has 23, 24, or 26 points.
    #Each team can get 24, 25, or 26 points per set.
    #The average is (24*3 + 25*2 + 26)/3
    points_per_set_average = (24*3 + 25*2 + 26)/3
    #The answer is
    result = points_per_set_average
    return result
Topic: football ### Response:  Question: A 12-person soccer team has 32 shirts. 
8 of the shirts are red. 
6 of the shirts are blue. 
The rest are white. 
How many white shirts are there?
Solution:
def solution():
    #A 12-person soccer team has 32 shirts
    total_shirts = 32
    #8 of the shirts are red
    red_shirts = 8
    #6 of the shirts are blue
    blue_shirts = 6
    #The rest are white. The answer is
    white_shirts = total_shirts - red_shirts - blue_shirts
    return white_shirts

Topic: ice cream ### Response:  Question: 
How many scoops of ice cream can you get from 1000 grams of cream?
Solution:
def solution():
    #1 scoop of ice cream is 250 grams of cream
    scoop_in_grams = 250
    #1000 grams of cream is
    cream_in_grams = 1000
    #The answer is
    result = cream_in_grams / scoop_in_grams
    return result

Topic: football ### Response:  Question: 11 players on the field. 22 players on the bench. 2000 fans in the stands. 
If 1/10 of the fans are wearing the home team's jersey, and 1/4 of the fans wearing the home team's jersey are also wearing the home team's hat, how many fans in the stands are wearing both the home team's jersey and the home team's hat?
Solution:
def solution():
    #11 players on the field
    field_players = 11
    #22 players on the bench
    bench_players = 22
    #2000 fans in the stands
    total_fans = 2000
    #1/10 of the fans are wearing the home team's jersey
    jersey_fans = total_fans / 10
    #1/4 of the fans wearing the home team's jersey are also wearing the home team's hat
    hat_fans = jersey_fans / 4
    #The answer is
    result = hat_fans
    return result
